# Engine-Capability Backlog v2 ŌĆö all cards faithful (2026-07)

**v1's 62 increments are all landed** ŌĆö see this file's git history for the full landed/skipped record of that wave. This is the v2 backlog, rebuilt from a fresh audit of the 259 cards that still carry `approximates`/dropped-clause notes after the v1 waves.

**The north star moved (ADR 0014): *every* card faithful. There are no non-goals anymore.** v1's "deliberate non-goals" (type-change layers, replacement/doubling engines, trigger-doubling, damage prevention, enter-as-copy) are now real increments ŌĆö honest XLs with staged first slices (#126ŌĆō#130). The method is unchanged: grow from real cards, TDD, smallest-increment-first, flag-don't-force.

**Effort scale** (unchanged from v1): S = one enum arm / deserializer field + one execute arm. M = a new struct or context plumbing touching 2ŌĆō3 modules. L = new state-machine surface (zones, choices, permissions). XL = subsystem, staged in slices.

Numbering continues from v1 (#63 onward) so wave briefs stay unambiguous. Rank = cards unblocked ├Ę effort, dependency prerequisites first. Every one of the 259 audited cards appears in at least one increment or the per-card exotics list.

---

## Tier 1 ŌĆö foundations and high-leverage wiring (build these first)

### 63. `color-filter-axis` ŌĆö 5 cards, M ŌĆö **LANDED (2026-07, partial pool)**
Cards have no color at all today ŌĆö the one characteristic axis the engine never modeled. Add a WUBRG mask to `CardDef` (derived from `Cost` pips at load, overridable for color-indicator cards), read by `PermanentFilter` (monocolored/multicolored/specific-color predicates), `Effect::AnthemStatic` ("other red creatures get +1/+1"), `SpellFilter` ("whenever you cast a white spell"), and `Condition` ("you control two or more white permanents"). Prereq for #64 (token color) and the Lieges' color-split anthems; Vanishing Verse's "monocolored permanent" is the cleanest first consumer.
*Cards:* balefire_liege, creakwood_liege, mistveil_plains, oran_rief_the_vastwood, vanishing_verse

**Landed:** added `ColorFilter` (`Any`/`Monocolored` only ŌĆö the pool's one consumer), a `color` axis on `PermanentFilter` (reads `Game::colors_of`, colorless correctly fails "exactly one color"), and `Condition::YouControlColorPermanents { color, at_least }` (activation gate). Fully faithful (note deleted): vanishing_verse ("exile target monocolored permanent"), mistveil_plains (tuck ability now gated on "two or more white permanents"). **Residual closed (2026-07):** `Effect::AnthemStatic` gained `colors`/`exclude_source` axes, `SpellFilter::Color`, and `color_identity` now reads hybrid pips (CR 105.2b); hybrid cast costs authored via the existing `Cost::hybrid`. Fully faithful (note deleted): creakwood_liege. balefire_liege's last residual ("or planeswalker" damage-target) closed 2026-07-16 ŌĆö now fully faithful (`target = "player_or_planeswalker"`, see #66's damage-to-planeswalker progress note). **Still blocked:** oran_rief_the_vastwood (mass filtered put-counters, not a color predicate).

### 64. `token-color-subtype` ŌĆö 23 cards, M ŌĆö depends on #63 ŌĆö **LANDED (2026-07, partial pool)**
Color and creature-subtype axes on token profiles: green Beast, black Rogue, white Cat/Pegasus, black-green Pest/Insect, blue-red Elemental, white Goat, blue Illusion. Token profiles are already full inline `CardDef`s (v1 #10), and creature subtypes landed in v1 #15 ŌĆö this is two fields on the inline def (`colors` from #63, `subtypes` which already exists on real cards but is never set on token profiles), consumed by the existing anthem/`PermanentFilter` subtype matching. Unblocks the Pest/Spirit/Saproling tribal payoffs whose anthem machinery already landed (Feral Appetite, Hofri).
*Cards:* ajanis_chosen, archon_of_suns_grace, beast_within, beledros_witherbloom, blight_mound, currency_converter, curse_of_the_swine, feral_appetite, forum_filibuster, furygale_flocking, hofri_ghostforge, intermediate_chirography, izoni, magma_opus, mycoloth, pawn_of_ulamog, pest_infestation, quintorius_field_historian, rapid_hybridization, resculpt, ribtruss_roaster, skyclave_apparition, woe_strider

**Landed:** `CardDef::colors` (`&'static [Color]`, empty = derive from cost pips as before), consulted by `color_identity` ahead of the cost-pip fallback; `colors`/`subtypes` on both token-profile shapes (the `power`/`toughness` sugar and the full inline-`CardDef` form) in `de.rs`; every listed token authored with its real color + creature subtype from Scryfall. Fully faithful (note deleted): archon_of_suns_grace (its own Pegasus token now also picks up the card's own lifelink anthem), beast_within, currency_converter, izoni, quintorius_field_historian, resculpt, woe_strider. Color/subtype-trimmed, residual note kept for an unrelated gap: ajanis_chosen (Aura-attach rider), beledros_witherbloom / mycoloth (token dies-ability / Devour), blight_mound (its own attacking-Pest anthem is dropped but ŌĆö noted as a followup ŌĆö now expressible with the already-landed `AnthemStatic` subtypes/attacking_only axes), curse_of_the_swine (X-scaling, #31/#58), forum_filibuster (Aura/Equipment reanimation rider), furygale_flocking (cost reduction, per-opponent scaling, forced-attack rider), intermediate_chirography (Class leveling, #133), magma_opus (damage-division/tap/alt-cost), pawn_of_ulamog (colorless Eldrazi Spawn ŌĆö subtype only; "nontoken" qualifier), rapid_hybridization (no-regeneration). **No token to color (whole ability dropped upstream, nothing minted):** feral_appetite (#116), hofri_ghostforge (death-trigger reanimation unmodeled), pest_infestation (body-only, no create_token at all), ribtruss_roaster (Devour/end-step generation dropped), skyclave_apparition (`Trigger::LeavesBattlefield`, #81).

**Progress (2026-07):** residual authoring pass on the tribal anthem / token dies-ability gaps this
entry flagged as followups ŌĆö `AnthemStatic`'s `subtypes`/`attacking_only`/`keywords` axes (already
landed) and the token-abilities pattern (already proven by blight_mound's own Pest) needed no engine
change, just authoring. Fully faithful (note deleted): beledros_witherbloom (its Pest token now
carries "When this token dies, you gain 1 life"). Anthem-trimmed, residual note kept for an
unrelated gap: blight_mound ("Attacking Pests you control get +1/+0 and have menace" now scripted;
residual is only the death trigger's dropped "nontoken" filter), feral_appetite ("Attacking Pests
you control get +1/+0 and have deathtouch" now scripted; residual is only the {1}{G} exile-a-
graveyard-card activated ability, which needs an exile-target-any-graveyard-card effect plus a
conditional "if a creature was exiled this way" payoff), hofri_ghostforge ("Spirits you control get
+1/+1 and have trample and haste" now scripted; residual is only the death-trigger reanimation,
which needs an exile-and-copy-on-death effect plus a subtype-add, #126, unlanded), pest_rescuer (its
Pest token's dies-ability and color now scripted; residual is only the lifegain-plus-1 replacement
effect, #128, unlanded, and the "each upkeep" ŌåÆ own-upkeep narrowing).

**Progress (2026-07-15) ŌĆö hofri_ghostforge's residual closed via #127's leaves-rider slice; now fully faithful.** The death-trigger exile-and-copy body (`Effect::ExileDeadCreatureCreateCopyWithSubtype`, #127 slices 1ŌĆō3b) and its Spirit token's granted leaves-battlefield return rider (#127's residual closure) are both landed ŌĆö hofri_ghostforge's `approximates` is deleted, no residual remains. Not #64's last non-faithful card: ajanis_chosen, blight_mound, curse_of_the_swine, forum_filibuster, furygale_flocking, intermediate_chirography, magma_opus, pawn_of_ulamog, rapid_hybridization, feral_appetite, pest_infestation, ribtruss_roaster, skyclave_apparition still carry residual/dropped-ability notes.

### 65. `amount-generalization-2` ŌĆö 29 cards, M ŌĆö **PARTIALLY LANDED (2026-07)**
The v1 #5 routing wave, round two: route `Amount` into the effect/cost sites still taking fixed ints (drain, mass pump, enters-with-counters, token count, draw, `grant_to_attached`, activation `pay_life`, `add_mana` repetition), and grow variants with real consumers ŌĆö `LifeGainedThisTurn` reads (the tally exists), turn-scoped creatures-entered/died counts (Gorma, Gyome), per-opponent-hand-card, `TargetPower` for StP's life, exiled card's MV, combat-damage-dealt and cast-spell-MV/X read from `TriggerContext` (the wiring v1 #16b deferred ŌĆö Deekah's Fractal, Prismari Pianist, Renegade Bull), a sacrificed creature's power recorded in the activation context (Dina), commander-color-count (Zimone), and a per-iteratee resolution for mass effects ("each creature deals damage to itself equal to its power", Wave of Reckoning). Each variant is one `Game::resolve_amount` arm once the routing is uniform ŌĆö the single biggest raw count in the v2 audit.
*Cards:* augusta_order_returned, blossoming_bogbeast, ceaseless_conflict, culling_ritual, deekah_fractal_theorist, defiling_daemogoth, dina_essence_brewer, dina_soul_steeper, eriette_of_the_charmed_apple, furygale_flocking, gorma_the_gullet, gyome_master_chef, hateful_eidolon, herald_of_amity, kor_spiritdancer, primo_the_unbounded, prismari_pianist, reanimate, renegade_bull, rousing_refrain, sages_reverie, skyclave_apparition, swords_to_plowshares, the_goose_mother, venerable_warsinger, volcanic_torrent, war_room, wave_of_reckoning, zimone_all_questioning
**Landed:** Part A routing ŌĆö `DrawCards`, `GainLife`, `EachOpponentDrain`, `EachOpponentLosesLife`, `CreateTokenCopy`, and `ActivationCost.pay_life` all take `Amount` now (behavior-preserving for existing `Fixed` cards). New `Amount` arms with live consumers: `CreaturesDiedThisTurn` (a turn-scoped tally mirroring `spells_cast_this_turn`), `SacrificedCreaturePower` (filled in from `Amount::Fixed` at ability-placement via the new `contextualize_sacrifice_effect`, mirroring how trigger context fills `AttackerDrawsControllerCounters`), `CommanderColorCount`. `DamageEachCreature`'s mass-effect loop now resolves its `Amount` per affected creature (source = that creature), so `Amount::SourcePower` reads each creature's own power with no new variant. Two new `Effect` variants: `LoseLife` (Reanimate's life-loss rider) and `GainLifeTargetController` (Swords to Plowshares' rider ŌĆö the *target's* controller, not the caster, gains life). Fully faithful (note deleted): dina_soul_steeper (sacrifice-pump ability), dina_essence_brewer (sacrifice gain-life/put-counters ability), wave_of_reckoning (per-iteratee self-damage), reanimate (mana-value life-loss rider), swords_to_plowshares (controller-gains-life rider). Trimmed: gorma_the_gullet (the death-tally amount is faithful, but only applied to Gorma's own entry ŌĆö the real ability grants counters to *every* nontoken creature you control entering, which needs a wider entering-permanent static the pool doesn't have yet), war_room (pay-life-as-commander-color-count landed; no other residual).
**Still blocked (untouched this round ŌĆö no unlanded prereq beyond scope):** augusta_order_returned, ceaseless_conflict, culling_ritual, deekah_fractal_theorist, furygale_flocking, gyome_master_chef (needs Food tokens, #78/#124), hateful_eidolon, herald_of_amity, kor_spiritdancer, primo_the_unbounded, prismari_pianist, renegade_bull, rousing_refrain, skyclave_apparition (needs `Trigger::LeavesBattlefield`, #81), the_goose_mother (Food, #78/#124), venerable_warsinger, volcanic_torrent, zimone_all_questioning (prime-count exotic) ŌĆö each needs cast/combat `TriggerContext` plumbing (deferred, #65 residual: "needs cast-spell-value in TriggerContext") or a different unlanded prereq named in its own note; not attempted this increment to keep the diff to the board/turn/activation-derived slice that lands cleanly.
**Progress (2026-07):** landed the "needs cast-spell-value in TriggerContext" residual named above.
`TriggerContext.cast_mana_value: Option<u32>`, filled only by `Game::queue_cast_spell_triggers`
from the cast `CardDef::mana_value()` (mirroring how `dying_source_stats` threads a dying source's
power into a `Dies` trigger). New placeholder `Amount::TriggeringSpellManaValue` and
`Condition::TriggeringSpellManaValueAtLeast { at_least }`, both baked to `Fixed`/resolved at trigger
placement by the new `fill_cast_mana_value` walker (CR 603.4 last-known-information, same shape as
`fill_dying_source_amounts`) ŌĆö never read live. Fully faithful (note deleted): prismari_pianist (the
"create three instead if mana value 5+" rider, via a `Sequence` + `Conditional` on `create_token`).
Trimmed: renegade_bull (the magecraft "+X/+0 where X is that spell's mana value" pump is now
faithful; residual is only the attack trigger's "exile up to one instant/sorcery from graveyard and
copy it, cast for free" ŌĆö needs graveyard-recast-from-exile support the pool lacks). **Still
blocked:** deekah_fractal_theorist needs a *variable-counter token* (0/0 Fractal with X +1/+1
counters, X = mana value) ŌĆö this thread supplies the MV read but not variable-counter tokens (#89
`variable-pt-tokens`); venerable_warsinger needs a *combat-damage-dealt* value plus a new "deals
combat damage to a player" trigger, a different `TriggerContext` thread this increment didn't touch.
**Progress (2026-07-11):** landed the board/turn-derived slice ŌĆö blossoming_bogbeast, defiling_daemogoth,
eriette_of_the_charmed_apple, sages_reverie. All four just needed authoring against `Amount`
routing that already existed (`LifeGainedThisTurn`, `PerPermanentMatching`,
`PumpCreaturesYouControlUntilEndOfTurn.power/.toughness`); the one engine change was widening
`Effect::GrantToAttached.power/.toughness` from `i32` to `Amount` (mirroring how #95 widened
`AnthemStatic`), resolved in `Game::attachment_grants` via `Game::resolve_amount` with the attached
Aura/Equipment as source and its controller as "you" ŌĆö Sage's Reverie's static half needed this to
read "Auras you control" live. Fully faithful (note deleted): blossoming_bogbeast (attack-triggered
life gain feeding a same-resolution team pump + trample), defiling_daemogoth (end-step drain scaled
by life gained this turn). Trimmed: sages_reverie (ETB draw and static +1/+1 both scale with a
`per_permanent` Aura count, but the filter has no "attached to a creature" axis so it counts every
Aura you control ŌĆö exact for this pool where every Aura enchants a creature); eriette_of_the_charmed_apple
(the end-step Aura-count drain is now scripted; residual is only the "enchanted creatures can't
attack you or your planeswalkers" restriction, which needs per-creature attack-declaration legality,
#80). Existing
`grant_to_attached` cards (Angelic Destiny, Bonesplitter, Sentinel's Eyes, the Impetus cycle, ŌĆ”)
reparse unchanged ŌĆö a bare int in TOML still deserializes to `Amount::Fixed(n)`.
**Progress (2026-07-11):** landed `Amount::PermanentsDestroyedThisWay { filter }` ŌĆö a "destroyed
this way" rider count (CR), scoped to *this resolution's own* `destroy_all` step rather than a
turn-wide tally: `Effect::DestroyAll`'s `resolve_effect` special case snapshots each destroyed
permanent's controller/token-ness/def onto a new `Game::destroyed_this_way` (overwritten, not
accumulated, on every `destroy_all` call), read back by the new `Amount` arm via a
`permanent_matches`-style filter over the snapshot. Both cards this slice named are now modeled
as `Sequence [destroy_all, rider]`. Fully faithful (note deleted): ceaseless_conflict (the
per-nontoken-creature-you-controlled Spirit-token rider ŌĆö `create_token` with `count = {
permanents_destroyed_this_way = { types = "creature", controller = "you", token = "nontoken" } }`)
and culling_ritual (the "{B} or {G}" mana rider ŌĆö `add_mana` with `mana = [["black", "green"]]`,
`repeat = { permanents_destroyed_this_way = {} }`). Culling Ritual's anticipated `{B}`-or-`{G}`
color-restriction residual didn't materialize: `Mana::Either(Black, Green)` ŌĆö the existing
dual-land "either of two colors, chosen at payment time" credit (already used by Llanowar Wastes
et al.) ŌĆö models the restricted-pair choice exactly, repeated `permanents_destroyed_this_way`
times via `AddMana.repeat`; no new mana-shape surface needed. **Not touched:** the rest of #65's
"still blocked" list (augusta_order_returned, deekah_fractal_theorist, furygale_flocking,
gyome_master_chef, hateful_eidolon, herald_of_amity, kor_spiritdancer, primo_the_unbounded,
prismari_pianist, rousing_refrain, skyclave_apparition, the_goose_mother, venerable_warsinger,
volcanic_torrent, zimone_all_questioning) ŌĆö each still needs its own separately-named prereq, not
this slice's count.
**Progress (2026-07-11):** landed `Amount::AurasAttachedToSource { auras_attached_to_source = {} }`
ŌĆö a live count of Auras (any controller) attached to the effect's source (CR 303.4), distinct from
the turn-scoped/controller-scoped `AurasYouControlledAttachedToDyingCreature`. Fully faithful (note
deleted): kor_spiritdancer (the "+2/+2 for each attached Aura" self-static ŌĆö two summed
+1/+1-per-Aura self-only anthems, the pool's doubled-anthem idiom ŌĆö plus the "cast an Aura ŌåÆ you
may draw" trigger, pure authoring against the already-landed `SpellFilter::Aura` cast trigger and
`optional`). **Not touched this slice:** the rest of #65's "not touched" list above.
**Progress (2026-07-11):** landed volcanic_torrent's opponent-scoped spell-count sweep. Added
`Effect::DamageEachCreature.opponents_only: bool` (mirroring `WeakenEachCreature`'s own axis) ŌĆö
`Amount::SpellsCastThisTurn` already existed, so the only missing primitive was the
opponents-only scope on the mass-damage sweep. Fully faithful minus Cascade (note trimmed):
volcanic_torrent ŌĆö the core "deals X damage to each creature ... your opponents control, X =
spells cast this turn" sweep now scripts exactly; residual note is only Cascade (no DSL form,
#132). The oracle's "and planeswalker" half is dropped via a `ponytail:` on the effect block
(mirrors #91's Mangara/Tomik planeswalker-attack gap ŌĆö no pool card fields a planeswalker
permanent to damage). Existing `damage_each_creature` cards (blasphemous_act, chain_reaction,
wave_of_reckoning) reparse unchanged ŌĆö no `opponents_only` key defaults to `false`. **Not
touched:** the rest of #65's "still blocked" list above.
**Progress (2026-07-11):** landed venerable_warsinger's residual ŌĆö the combat-damage-dealt value
plus the "deals combat damage to a player" trigger, per that entry's own note above. New
`TriggerContext.combat_damage: Option<i32>`, filled only by `Game::queue_combat_damage_triggers`
(now threading the source event's `amount`) for the `who = "this"` watcher, mirroring how
`cast_mana_value` threads a cast spell's MV into a `CastSpell` trigger. New placeholder
`CardFilter::CreatureWithManaValueAtMostCombatDamage`, baked to `CreatureWithManaValueAtMost` at
trigger placement by the new `fill_combat_damage` walker (CR 510.2/603.10a last-known information,
same shape as `fill_dying_source_amounts`) ŌĆö never matched live. The ability is authored `optional
= true` (CR "you may return"), so an empty graveyard fizzles harmlessly on accept rather than
forcing an action. Fully faithful (note deleted): venerable_warsinger. This also clears the
venerable_warsinger entry under #69 (`graveyard-card-filters-2`), which named the same "deals
combat damage to a player" trigger as its blocker. **Still blocked (untouched this round):**
augusta_order_returned, ceaseless_conflict's remaining residual (if any), culling_ritual,
deekah_fractal_theorist (needs #89 variable-pt-tokens, per the note above), furygale_flocking,
gyome_master_chef, hateful_eidolon, herald_of_amity, primo_the_unbounded (needs a batched
base-power-0-filtered combat-damage trigger + summed damage + `{X}{X}` cost, #68 ŌĆö a bigger slice
than this single-creature `who = "this"` bake), prismari_pianist, rousing_refrain, skyclave_apparition,
the_goose_mother, zimone_all_questioning.
**Progress (2026-07-12):** landed the Food-token-sacrifice-family slice ŌĆö gyome_master_chef's own
blocker premise ("Food is an artifact token the pool can't mint yet") was already false
(gilded_goose mints a working Food profile); what was missing was a non-creature sacrifice cost and
a turn-scoped nontoken-creatures-entered count, both now supplied by #78's sibling progress note.
New `Amount::NontokenCreaturesEnteredThisTurn` (`Player::nontoken_creatures_entered_this_turn`,
reset at Untap, bumped once per entering permanent in `Game::queue_permanent_enters_triggers` when
it's a nontoken creature ŌĆö mirrors `CreaturesDiedThisTurn` exactly). Also fixed a latent gap this
slice's TDD surfaced: a self `Trigger::Etb` ability's `Amount::X`/`HalfX` reads resolved as 0 (the
"abilities carry no X" default) because nothing filled `TriggerContext.cast_x` for it ŌĆö extended
`Game::queue_self_trigger` (used only by `Trigger::Etb`) to fill `cast_x` from the entering
permanent's own already-placed `+1/+1` counters (the same X proxy `Game::ability_source_x` already
used for Kinetic Ooze's `mv_max_x`), and added the missing `Amount::HalfX` arm to `fill_cast_x`
(only `X`/`HalfXRoundedDown` were wired). Fully faithful (notes deleted): the_goose_mother (ETB
"create half X Food tokens" + attack-trigger "may sacrifice a Food, draw a card" ŌĆö pure authoring
once the X-fill fix landed; no card in the pool previously had an ETB ability reading `Amount::X`,
so this was a real gap, not a documentation-only fix), gyome_master_chef (end-step Food count +
"{1}, Sacrifice a Food: target creature gains indestructible until end of turn, tap it" ŌĆö the tap
step shares the pump step's chosen target by both declaring the same `target = "creature"` spec,
the established idiom, per Killian, Decisive Mentor's tap-then-goad). Also fully faithful as a
bonus #78 consumer: gilded_goose ("{T}, Sacrifice a Food: Add one mana of any color", its last
residual). **Still not touched:** the rest of this entry's "still blocked" list above
(gyome_master_chef and the_goose_mother now cleared from it).
**Progress (2026-07-12):** landed furygale_flocking's per-opponent scaling, its only residual under
this entry. `Effect::CreateToken`'s `TokenController::OnePerOpponent` recipient list now pairs each
opponent with its own must-attack defender (`Vec<(PlayerId, Option<PlayerId>)>` batches, replacing
the flat `recipients` + single `required_defender`), so each opponent's own pair of minted tokens is
forced to attack *that* opponent, not one flattened opponent shared by every token. Every other
`controller` value (`you`/`target_controller`/`each_opponent`/`target_player`) keeps today's
flattened single-opponent defender unchanged. Fully faithful (note + ponytail header deleted):
furygale_flocking. **Still blocked (untouched this round):** augusta_order_returned,
ceaseless_conflict's remaining residual (if any), culling_ritual, deekah_fractal_theorist (needs #89
variable-pt-tokens), hateful_eidolon, herald_of_amity, primo_the_unbounded (needs #68), prismari_pianist,
rousing_refrain, skyclave_apparition, zimone_all_questioning.
**Progress (2026-07-14):** landed deekah_fractal_theorist's dropped second ability. The prior
"needs #89 variable-pt-tokens" note was stale on both counts: the Magecraft token already scripted
its X +1/+1 counters via the pre-existing `enters_with = "triggering_spell_mana_value"`, and the
"{3}{U}: target creature token can't be blocked this turn" ability needed no new machinery either ŌĆö
`Effect::PumpUntilEndOfTurn` + `Keyword::Unblockable` + the inline `target = { permanent = { token =
"token" } }` filter (all already used by other cards) cover it exactly. Fully faithful (note
deleted): deekah_fractal_theorist. **Still blocked (untouched this round):** augusta_order_returned,
ceaseless_conflict's remaining residual (if any), culling_ritual, hateful_eidolon, herald_of_amity,
primo_the_unbounded (needs #68), prismari_pianist, rousing_refrain, skyclave_apparition,
zimone_all_questioning.
**Progress (2026-07-15):** landed gorma_the_gullet's last-named residual ŌĆö the third ability's
entering-permanent-wide static grant. New `Effect::CreaturesYouControlEnterWithCounters { filter,
count }` (the *other*-permanent-wide sibling of `EntersWithCounters`, CR 614.1c): a battlefield
static that watches every permanent its controller casts, applied at the ETB counter choke in
`Game::resolve_spell` via a new `Game::additional_enter_counters(entered, controller)` scan ŌĆö
sums every qualifying static's resolved `count` over the controller's *other* permanents. A
static never modifies its own permanent's entry (Master Biomancer / Corpsejack Menace ruling ŌĆö the
static isn't functioning until the permanent is on the battlefield), so Gorma herself no longer
enters with these counters; the old self-only `enters_with_counters` authoring over-counted her own
entry. Wired only at the cast-resolution choke ŌĆö reanimation/blink entries don't get the bonus (no
pool card observes that gap). Fully faithful (note + ponytail header deleted): gorma_the_gullet. **Still blocked
(untouched this round):** augusta_order_returned, ceaseless_conflict's remaining residual (if
any), culling_ritual, hateful_eidolon, herald_of_amity, primo_the_unbounded (needs #68),
prismari_pianist, rousing_refrain, skyclave_apparition, zimone_all_questioning.
**Progress (2026-07-15):** landed zimone_all_questioning's end-step trigger, the last of #65's
"still blocked" cards. Three additions: `Condition::All { conditions }` (a composed AND ŌĆö
`Ability.condition` is a single slot, and Zimone needs two ANDed intervening-ifs), a landfall
history flag `Player::land_entered_under_your_control_this_turn` (set at the same
permanent-enters choke `nontoken_creatures_entered_this_turn` bumps at, for any land ŌĆö cast,
fetched, or token; reset each untap), and `Condition::YouControlPrimeNumberOfLands` (a small
trial-division `is_prime` over `Game::lands_controlled`). The token itself was already
expressible ŌĆö `create_token` with an inline legendary token profile and `enters_with = {
per_permanent = { types = "land", controller = "you" } }` (routed through the existing #89
`counters_after_replacements` pipeline) mints Primo with "that many" +1/+1 counters directly, no
separate counter-placement step needed. Fully faithful (note + ponytail header deleted):
zimone_all_questioning. **Still blocked (untouched this round):** augusta_order_returned,
ceaseless_conflict's remaining residual (if any), culling_ritual, hateful_eidolon,
herald_of_amity, primo_the_unbounded (needs #68), prismari_pianist, rousing_refrain,
skyclave_apparition.
**Progress (2026-07-15, rider):** closed kinetic_ooze ŌĆö the XŌēź10 "double the number of +1/+1
counters on any number of other target creatures" rider its `approximates` note flagged (it named
#73's one-target-clause-per-ability limit as the blocker). Landed alongside #73's multi-clause work
this same day: the ETB already carried the destroy target (placement-time) and the XŌēź5 draw; the
third clause is a new no-target-of-its-own effect `double_counters_on_chosen_creatures`, gated by
`conditional { source_entered_with_x_at_least = 10 }`, that pauses at resolution (ponytail CR 603.3d)
on a new `PendingChoice::DoubleCountersTargets` to pick any number of other creatures and doubles
each ŌĆö the same resolution-time any-subset shape `phase_out` uses. This sidesteps threading a
per-clause target list onto the `Copy` `StackItem::Ability`. **Trimmed to one residual:**
kinetic_ooze ŌĆö enters with X counters, ETB destroys up to one MVŌēżX artifact/enchantment, draws at
XŌēź5, and doubles chosen other creatures' counters at XŌēź10, all as one triggered ability. The
`approximates` note is trimmed (not deleted) to the residual: "other **target** creatures" is a
non-targeted resolution-time subset choice (CR 603.3d), so shroud/hexproof/protection aren't
enforced and responders can't react to the specific set. See #73's 2026-07-15 note for the shared
machinery.
**Progress (2026-07-16):** landed rousing_refrain's persistent-mana residual ŌĆö CR 500.4's "until
end of turn, you don't lose this mana as steps and phases end." New
`Effect::AddMana.persist_until_end_of_turn` (TOML `persist_until_end_of_turn = true`) threads onto a
new `Event::ManaAdded.persist` flag, which mirrors the credit into a new `Player::persistent_mana`
side-pool alongside the ordinary `mana_pool` (payment/spend path untouched). `Event::ManaEmptied`
grew an `end_of_turn` flag (set only when leaving Cleanup): a mid-turn step/phase boundary keeps
`mana_pool.componentwise_min(&persistent_mana)` in both pools (a spent persistent credit doesn't
resurrect), while the turn actually ending (CR 514.2) clears both. **Fully faithful (note + ponytail
header deleted):** rousing_refrain. **Still blocked (untouched this round):** augusta_order_returned,
ceaseless_conflict's remaining residual (if any), culling_ritual, hateful_eidolon, herald_of_amity,
primo_the_unbounded (needs #68), prismari_pianist, skyclave_apparition.

### 66. `target-filter-adoption` ŌĆö 18 cards, S ŌĆö **LANDED (2026-07)**
Wire the landed composable `PermanentFilter` into the targeted effects still using narrow specs: `put_counters` ("artifact or creature you control"), `deal_damage` (creature-or-planeswalker), `destroy` (enchantment-only / artifact-or-enchantment / land), `bounce`, `CreateTokenCopy` ("permanent you control"), `destroy_all` (planeswalkers/battles ŌĆö battles need the type added to `TypeSet`), plus small missing axes: power-parity for mass bounce (Zimone's Hypothesis), a card-name filter (Leitmotif Composer), mv_max on targeted removal. Pure data-plumbing and authoring ŌĆö no new subsystem; the filter struct already carries most of these fields.
*Cards:* casualties_of_war, final_act, kami_of_ancient_law, kinetic_ooze, leitmotif_composer, ozolith_the_shattered_spire, prismari_command, quandrix_charm, quandrix_command, replication_technique, rip_apart, steelbane_hydra, vanishing_verse, volcanic_salvo, white_orchid_phantom, witherbloom_charm, witherbloom_command, zimones_hypothesis
**Landed:** added `Parity` + `PermanentFilter.power_parity` (zero-is-even) and three `_or_` type-union shorthands. Fully faithful (note deleted): kami_of_ancient_law, steelbane_hydra, ozolith_the_shattered_spire (its counter-replacement is already type-agnostic over the controller's permanents ŌĆö a pool-faithful superset of "artifact or creature"), replication_technique (any-permanent-you-control copy). Trimmed to a precise residual: prismari_command (artifact destroy), quandrix_charm (enchantment), quandrix_command (creature-or-planeswalker bounce), witherbloom_command/witherbloom_charm (nonland + mv_max), rip_apart (artifact-or-enchantment), white_orchid_phantom (ETB land destroy, optional), zimones_hypothesis (modal odd/even mass bounce).
**Still blocked:** casualties_of_war/final_act + battle-type cards (need modal "choose one or more"/battle `TypeSet`), leitmotif_composer (card-name filter), vanishing_verse (color axis #63), kinetic_ooze (X-value filters #99), volcanic_salvo (multi-target #73/#85).
**Progress (2026-07-16):** closed rip_apart's residual ŌĆö damage to a planeswalker (CR 120.3c/306.9) is
now modeled: `Effect::DealDamage`'s `Target::Object` branch checks `CardKind::Planeswalker` ahead of
the Tajic noncombat-damage guard and emits `Event::LoyaltyChanged { amount: -amount }` instead of
`DamageMarked` (the 0-loyalty SBA already destroys it ŌĆö no new event/pending choice). Two new
`TargetSpec` unit variants carry this to the target-enumeration side (`query.rs`'s `legal_targets_for`,
reusing the `ArtifactEnchantmentOrPlaneswalker` battlefield-scan shape via a new `planeswalkers`
closure): `CreatureOrPlaneswalker` (`"creature_or_planeswalker"`) and `PlayerOrPlaneswalker`
(`"player_or_planeswalker"`). `TargetSpec::AnyTarget` (`"any"`, CR 115.4) now also chains
`planeswalkers()` ŌĆö its ponytail is trimmed to the one remaining gap (battles aren't a modeled
permanent type). **Fully faithful (note deleted):** rip_apart (mode 0 is now
`target = "creature_or_planeswalker"`). This also closed the pool's other two "or planeswalker"
notes, though neither is one of this entry's 18 cards: balefire_liege (`#66` cousin ŌĆö the
cast-a-red-spell trigger is now `target = "player_or_planeswalker"`) and magma_opus's divided-damage
residual (`#73`'s `target = "any"` reaches planeswalkers for free now that `AnyTarget` does ŌĆö see
#73's own progress log; its `approximates` line, which cited "(#91)", is deleted). Quintorius, History
Chaser (`crates/cards/data/quintorius_history_chaser.toml`) is the pool's only planeswalker and the
live target proven by all three cards' new engine tests. **Follow-up noted, not built:** planeswalkers
still can't be *attacked* ŌĆö that's a separate, larger combat-defender slice, out of this increment's
scope.

Also thread the triggering spell into `TriggerContext` so a payoff can copy it (Owlin) or gate an anthem (Nev).
*Cards:* brass_infiniscope, decisive_denial, dirgur_focusmage, elementalists_palette, lattice_library, nev_the_practical_dean, owlin_spiralmancer, quandrix_command, sram_senior_edificer, starfield_mystic, teshar_ancestors_apostle, unbound_flourishing, zimone_infinite_analyst

Trimmed: quandrix_command (mode-1 counter now artifact-or-enchantment; residual is the mode-4 graveyard shuffle #105), starfield_mystic (reducer now enchantment-only ŌĆö including Auras via type-bit check; residual is the enchantment-dies +1/+1 trigger #81).

### 68. `x-in-costs-full` ŌĆö 7 cards, M ŌĆö **LANDED (2026-07-12)**
Full X plumbing, the open slices of v1 #58: `Cost.x` bool ŌåÆ u8 multiplier so `{X}{X}` pays double (Hangarback enters at half size today; Astral Cornucopia's `{X}{X}{X}`), X as an effect/target count ("exile X creatures", "top X of library" ŌĆö wired past `return_to_hand` via #73's `TargetCount`), and X carried into the `SpellCast` trigger context ("whenever you cast a spell with `{X}`", "gain half X"). `Amount::X`/`TwiceX`/`HalfX` already exist on the effect side ŌĆö this is the cost and context half.
*Cards:* animists_awakening, astral_cornucopia, brass_infiniscope, curse_of_the_swine, hangarback_walker, pest_infestation, primo_the_unbounded
**Progress (2026-07):** landed the first slice ŌĆö `Cost.x: bool ŌåÆ u8` cost multiplier (CR 107.3: every
`{X}` in a cost is the same chosen value, paid once per symbol). `Cost::with_x` now multiplies the
chosen X by the pip count before folding into `generic`, with the same saturating clamp guard as
before (a huge X still can't wrap to a cheap cost). `de.rs`'s `[cost]` table's `x` key accepts either
`x = true` (ŌåÆ multiplier 1, every other pool card's spelling, unchanged) or an integer `x = N`
(ŌåÆ multiplier N), via a small untagged `XPips` bool-or-u8 helper ŌĆö no TOML migration forced.
`schema::catalog::wire_cost`'s `has_x` is now `cost.x > 0`. Fully faithful (note deleted):
astral_cornucopia (`{X}{X}{X}`, enters with X charge counters, taps for one mana per counter ŌĆö the
cost was the only residual). Trimmed to a precise residual: hangarback_walker (`{X}{X}` cost now
faithful; still approximated on the die-trigger Thopter swarm ŌĆö `create_token`'s count can't scale
off +1/+1 counters, a separate gap). Every other `x = true` card in the pool (animists_awakening,
curse_of_the_swine, pest_infestation, primo_the_unbounded, reanimate, ŌĆ”) is unaffected ŌĆö proven by a
behavior-preserving test (`single_x_spell_still_pays_x_once`) that a multiplier-1 `{X}` card still
pays X exactly once.
**Still deferred (not attempted in the first pass ŌĆö the target-count half landed in the second pass
below; do NOT mark #68 LANDED):** X carried into the `SpellCast` trigger context
(brass_infiniscope's "next spell cast with {X}, draw half X cards" delayed trigger; primo_the_unbounded
likely also needs this), which touches delayed-trigger-context machinery out of scope for those passes'
diff size.
**Progress (2026-07-11):** landed the second slice ŌĆö X as an effect/target count (CR 601.2b/601.2c).
`TargetCount` gained an `x_scaled: bool` (`#[serde(default)]`); `Game::choose_spell_targets`
(cast.rs, the one choke point every multi-target spell/copy-retarget already routes through)
substitutes the spell's own chosen X for a placeholder `min`/`max` before the legal-target clamp:
`{ min: 0, max: 0, x_scaled: true }` is "up to X target(s)" (Silkguard), `{ min: 1, max: 1,
x_scaled: true }` is "exactly X target(s)" (Curse of the Swine), both capped at `MAX_TARGETS` (a
named ponytail, not exercised by any pool card). `TargetCount::is_single()` now also gates on
`!x_scaled` so an X-scaled `{1,1}` still routes through the multi-target machinery instead of the
single-target fast path. `Effect::ExileTarget` and `Effect::DestroyTarget` each gained a `count:
TargetCount` (`#[serde(default)]`, behavior-preserving for every existing single-target card).
**Fully faithful (notes deleted):** silkguard's target *count* (residual trimmed to the unrelated
#90 "modified creatures gain hexproof" rider only); curse_of_the_swine (exile X target creatures,
*and* the "for each creature exiled this way, its controller creates a 2/2 Boar" rider ŌĆö the
existing multi-target expansion in `resolve_spell` already re-runs a `Sequence`'s whole per-target
resolution once per chosen target, so the per-target Boar rider fell out for free, no extra wiring
needed ŌĆö a pleasant surprise past what this slice's own sketch assumed would stay dropped);
pest_infestation (both halves: "destroy up to X target artifacts and/or enchantments" via the new
`DestroyTarget.count`, and "create twice X ... Pest tokens" via the already-existing
`Amount::TwiceX`, reusing blight_mound.toml's proven "dies: gain 1 life" token-ability shape
verbatim). pest_infestation's two clauses are **not** a per-target `Sequence`, unlike Curse of the
Swine's ŌĆö the token count must fire exactly once regardless of how many permanents were actually
destroyed, so it's a second, untargeted `[[abilities]]` block instead (documented in
`DSL_REFERENCE.md` ┬¦5, the `Sequence`-per-target-vs-separate-`[[abilities]]` split). **Still
blocked, untouched:** immoral_bargain ŌĆö its X must drive a sacrifice *additional cost* and target a
"nonland permanent," neither of which this slice touches; X carried into the `SpellCast` trigger
context (brass_infiniscope, primo_the_unbounded) is unattempted, the one remaining #68 slice ŌĆö do
NOT mark #68 LANDED.
**Progress (2026-07-11):** landed the "cast a spell with {X} in its mana cost"/"cast a historic
spell" trigger slice. Two new `SpellFilter` arms: `HasXInCost` (`"has_x"` ŌĆö `def.cost.x > 0`, CR

this-turn cast tally) is the newly-surfaced engine gap ŌĆö Nev/Zimone are the first cards to pair

**Progress (2026-07-11):** landed the filtered `nth_each_turn` gate ŌĆö the newly-surfaced gap from
the previous note. `Player` gained `x_spells_cast_this_turn: u32`, a filter-scoped sibling of

its `enters_with_counters` count flipped from the single-`x` `"x"` spelling to the already-existing

qualifying attacker, not once per source. `Game::queue_zero_base_power_combat_damage_triggers`
scans the just-applied event batch's `CombatDamageDealtToPlayer`s for BASE-power-0 sources (read
off `def_of(source).kind`, not `Game::power`, so a counter-pumped Fractal still counts), sums by

each controller's watcher once per defending player. A new placeholder `Amount::CombatDamageDealt`
(`"combat_damage_dealt"`) plus a `fill_combat_damage` arm on `Effect::CreateToken` locks the
minted Fractal's `enters_with` to the summed damage at trigger placement (CR 603.10a last-known

`DealsCombatDamageToPlayer`'s reanimation-target fill already threads. **Fully faithful (note and

now faithful. A new `Effect::RevealTopCards` (`reveal_top_cards`), `RevealUntil`'s sibling: reveals
exactly the top `count` cards (not "until N match"), CR 120.3 "as many as possible" on a short
library, every match to `matched_dest`/`matched_tapped`, every other revealed card to `rest_dest`
(bottom, same deterministic library-order stand-in for CR 701.19's "random order" `reveal_until`
already uses ŌĆö no `rand` in the pure engine). Spell mastery ("If there are two or more instant
and/or sorcery cards in your graveyard, untap those lands") is modeled as a new
`deploy_untapped_if: Option<Condition>` field gating `matched_tapped` at resolution, backed by a new
`Condition::InstantOrSorceryCardsInYourGraveyardAtLeast`: "enters tapped, then untap those lands"
and "enters untapped" are observably identical (nothing can respond to the intermediate tapped
state before the untap resolves as part of the same effect), so this bakes the net result in
directly rather than modeling a separate untap step. **Fully faithful (note deleted):**
animists_awakening. **#68 LANDED ŌĆö every card faithful, no residuals.**

### 69. `graveyard-card-filters-2` ŌĆö 13 cards, M ŌĆö **LANDED (2026-07-14)**
Widen graveyard targeting past creature cards, on the landed `TargetSpec::CardInGraveyard`/`CardFilter` shapes: reanimate artifact-or-creature (Lorehold Charm mode 2), artifact (Restore Relic), nonland permanent MV-gated (Guardian Scalelord, Sun Titan, Primary Research), Aura/Equipment (Forum Filibuster), Excava's "artifact, creature, or non-Aura enchantment" exclusion, `whose: Any` on reanimate (Karmic Guide), instant-or-sorcery + a top-of-library tuck destination (Mystic Sanctuary ŌĆö `TuckFromGraveyard` landed bottom-only), return-a-land-to-hand (Witherbloom Command mode 0), and `mass_return_from_graveyard{filter}` for Replenish (Eiganjo's back face). Mostly filter arms + one mass variant over the landed reanimate event path (Sevinne's Reclamation proves the shape).
*Cards:* eiganjo_dynastorian, excava_the_risen_past, forum_filibuster, guardian_scalelord, karmic_guide, lorehold_archivist, lorehold_charm, mystic_sanctuary, primary_research, sun_titan, surge_to_victory, venerable_warsinger, witherbloom_command

**Progress (2026-07):** landed five new `CardFilter` arms (`NonlandPermanentWithManaValueAtMost`,
`ArtifactOrCreatureWithManaValueAtMost`, `ArtifactCreatureOrNonAuraEnchantmentWithManaValueAtMost`,
`InstantOrSorcery`, `Enchantment`), a `to_top: bool` on `TuckFromGraveyard` (default `false` =
existing bottom behavior) plus the matching field on `Event::TuckedToLibrary`, a new
`Effect::MassReturnFromGraveyard { filter }` looping the reanimate event path over every matching
graveyard card, and a new `Condition::ThisPermanentEnteredUntapped` (source-object-based like
`SourceHasCounters`; `Game::queue_trigger_group` special-cases it against its own `source` param
via a new `ability_condition_holds` wrapper, since `TriggerContext` carries no source id either).
Fully faithful (note deleted): sun_titan, primary_research, lorehold_charm, karmic_guide,
mystic_sanctuary. Trimmed to a precise residual: excava_the_risen_past (only the dynamic-P/T
Spirit type-change, #126, remains ŌĆö the graveyard filter itself is now exact), eiganjo_dynastorian
(the Replenish back face's own effect is now expressible via `mass_return_from_graveyard`, proven
by a standalone test, but the card stays blocked on DFC/prepare authoring, #77, to reach it).
(witherbloom_command's mode-0 status as of this pass is superseded by the 2026-07-11 progress
note below.)

**Progress (2026-07-11):** landed witherbloom_command mode 0 in full ŌĆö the prior note's
"two-independent-targets gap" framing was wrong; empirically, `Effect::Sequence`'s existing
"a step with no target of its own reads the enclosing target" rule already covers this exactly.
Mode 0 is now `Sequence { Mill { target: player }, MayReturnFromGraveyard { filter: Land } }`:
the mill shares the mode's chosen player target, and the untargeted `MayReturnFromGraveyard` step
ignores it, pausing on the caster's own graveyard instead ŌĆö no engine change, pure TOML (proven
by `witherbloom_command_mode_0_mills_then_returns_land` in `crates/engine/tests/game.rs`, plus a
modal-loop precedent already exercised by `prismari_command_mode_one_...`'s mid-resolution pause).
**Fully faithful (note deleted): witherbloom_command** ŌĆö all four modes now exact. Residual:
oracle's "you return" (mandatory) is modeled as "you may return" (`ponytail:` on the ability) ŌĆö
declining is illegal by the letter of the card but returning a land is pure upside, so the
divergence is unobservable; upgrade path is a mandatory `ReturnACardFromYourGraveyard { filter }`
sibling if a future card ever punishes declining.
**Still blocked:** forum_filibuster
(Aura/Equipment attachment rider), surge_to_victory (noncreature graveyard target + delayed copy,
multiple unlanded verbs), lorehold_archivist (prepare face, #77) ŌĆö each needs a different unlanded
prereq, not attempted this pass. Do NOT mark #69 LANDED. (forum_filibuster's status here is
superseded by the 2026-07-12 progress note below; guardian_scalelord's by the 2026-07-14 note.)
**Progress (2026-07-11):** venerable_warsinger's "combat-damage-to-player recursion trigger" is
landed via #65's `combat_damage`/`fill_combat_damage` thread (see that entry) ŌĆö fully faithful,
note deleted. Cleared from this entry's still-blocked list.

**Progress (2026-07-12):** forum_filibuster's Aura/Equipment attachment rider landed. New
`Effect::ReanimateAttachedToMintedToken { filter }`: reads back the token the same `effects`
sequence's preceding `create_token` step just minted (the `AttachTriggeringAuraToMintedToken`
read-back idiom), then pauses on a resolution-time-scoped `PendingChoice`
(`ReanimateAttachedToMintedToken`, reusing `Intent::ChooseSacrifices`'s "empty declines, one entry
picks" wire shape like `MayReturnFromGraveyard`) over the controller's own graveyard cards matching
`filter` ŌĆö an empty answer or empty graveyard is a legal no-op, and critically the pause is scoped
to just this step, so a declined/empty return never cancels the token the ability already minted
(unlike the shared `TargetSpec`-driven trigger-placement path, which drops the whole ability on an
empty/declined "up to one"). forum_filibuster is trimmed, not deleted: CR 603.3b's "when you do" is
really a separate triggered ability with its own stack object and priority window; this models it
as a same-resolution sequenced payoff instead (the same shortcut Augusta, Order Returned's
reflexive counter payoff already takes) ŌĆö no response window between the token's creation and the
return-and-attach.
**Progress (2026-07-15) ŌĆö forum_filibuster now fully faithful; residual closed.** The reflexive
"when you do" is a real CR 603.3b stack object (see the reflexive-trigger bullet in Per-card
exotics, LANDED 2026-07-15): `Effect::ReanimateAttachedToMintedToken` is replaced by
`Effect::ReflexiveTrigger { then }` (the reusable primitive ŌĆö enqueues its `then` as a separate,
respondable triggered ability via the normal APNAP placement path) + its body
`Effect::ReturnFromGraveyardAttachedToToken` (a real `CardInGraveyard` "up to one" target chosen at
placement, CR 601.2c). The old resolution-time `PendingChoice::ReanimateAttachedToMintedToken` and
its schema mirror are deleted. `approximates` deleted ŌĆö forum_filibuster fully faithful.
**Still blocked, each a distinct unlanded prereq:** surge_to_victory (noncreature graveyard target
+ delayed copy, multiple unlanded verbs), lorehold_archivist (prepare/DFC front face, #77). Do NOT
mark #69 LANDED.
**Progress (2026-07-14, via #123):** guardian_scalelord fully faithful ŌĆö its reanimation gained the
nonland-permanent breadth + the MV-X-or-less graveyard gate (X = its power, `NonlandPermanentWith
ManaValueAtMostSourcePower` baked at attack-trigger placement) alongside the landed Backup grant.
`approximates` deleted; cleared from this entry's blocked lists.

consumer of the same landed graveyard-filter surface) adopted the structured `card_in_graveyard`
reanimation target, closing its ETB gap. Its oracle reads "target permanent card with mana value 4
or less" ŌĆö the same construction as sun_titan's, not primary_research's "**nonland** permanent

not the nonland variant. Fully faithful except Encore: `approximates` trimmed to "Encore is dropped
(no encore keyword / token-copy-per-opponent, #127)." No engine change; pure TOML retarget.

blocker (#77) is now landed, proven end to end by striding_shotcaller/eiganjo_dynastorian. New
`Condition::ArtifactOrCreatureCardsInYourGraveyardAtLeast { count }` backs the front face's
upkeep intervening-if (sibling of `InstantOrSorceryCardsInYourGraveyardAtLeast`); new
`Effect::ExileTargetFromGraveyardCreateTokenCopy { filter }` and `CardFilter::ArtifactOrCreature`
back Restore Relic's body ŌĆö exile the targeted graveyard card, then mint a token copy of its
copiable characteristics (CR 707.2), the graveyard-target twin of `Effect::CreateTokenCopy`.
**Still blocked:** surge_to_victory (noncreature graveyard target + delayed copy, multiple unlanded
verbs) ŌĆö the only remaining card on this entry. Do NOT mark #69 LANDED.

**Progress (2026-07-14):** surge_to_victory fully faithful (`approximates` deleted) ŌĆö the last
card on this entry. New `Effect::ExileTargetGraveyardCardRecordManaValue { filter }` (a targeted
sibling of `ExileTargetGraveyardSpellAndCopyFree` that exiles without minting a copy, snapshotting
the exiled card's id + mana value onto a new resolution-scoped `Game::surge_exiled_card`, the
`milled_mana_value_this_way` idiom) backs "exile target instant or sorcery card from your
graveyard"; a new `Amount::ExiledCardManaValueThisWay` feeds the already-landed
`PumpCreaturesYouControlUntilEndOfTurn` (#65) for the team +X/+0; a new
`Effect::ScheduleThisTurnCombatDamageCopy` arms a CR 603.7 delayed watch
(`DelayedTriggers::pending_combat_damage_copy`) ŌĆö controller-scoped (any creature you control, not
one chosen creature) and **repeatable** for the rest of the turn, unlike `ArmCombatDamageWatch`'s
one-shot single-creature/single-combat shape ŌĆö draining through a new
`Game::fire_combat_damage_copy_triggers` pipeline phase that mints a free copy
(`Effect::MintFreeCopyOfExiledCard`) via the existing `mint_spell_copies` machinery each time a
qualifying creature connects, cleared unconsumed at the next turn's Untap (mirrors
`pending_next_cast`'s turn-boundary clear). **This also clears surge_to_victory from #74's and
#65's still-blocked lists** (both entries stay open ŌĆö other cards remain there).

### 70. `permanent-filter-axes-wiring` ŌĆö 11 cards, S ŌĆö **LANDED (2026-07, partial pool)**
`PermanentFilter` already carries `other: bool` and `token: TokenFilter` ŌĆö but anthems, counter replacements, and the watch-trigger scans don't consult them. Wire `other` (Lieges' "other creatures", Benevolent Hydra's counter-doubling excluding itself) and `token`/nontoken ("creature tokens you control have haste", "nontoken creature dies", "target token") through `matching_anthems`, `counters_after_replacements`, and the dies/enters watch filters; add the two missing axes: an entered-this-turn timestamp on `Permanent` (Oran-Rief's "each green creature that entered this turn", Redoubled Stormsinger's copy set) and an is-commander flag ("commander creatures you control get +2/+2", Guardian Augmenter ŌĆö one filter field, the keyword-granting anthem already landed).
*Cards:* balefire_liege, benevolent_hydra, blight_mound, brudiclad_telchor_engineer, creakwood_liege, deekah_fractal_theorist, guardian_augmenter, oran_rief_the_vastwood, pawn_of_ulamog, perplexing_test, redoubled_stormsinger

**Landed:** `Effect::AnthemStatic` gained `commander_only: bool` (gated on `Game::is_commander` in `matching_anthems`); `Effect::CounterReplacement` gained `other: bool` (`counters_after_replacements` now enumerates with index and skips the replacement when its own source is the receiver). Fully faithful (note deleted): guardian_augmenter (both statics are commander_only anthems ŌĆö +2/+2 and hexproof; one honest `// ponytail:` left noting creature-scoped anthem is exact for the pool since every commander is a creature). Fully faithful (note deleted): benevolent_hydra (counter-doubler excludes its own counters; the `{T}` ability's remove-a-+1/+1-counter cost and its "another" self-exclusion both now modeled ŌĆö see `remove-counter-cost` exotic increment). balefire_liege, creakwood_liege closed by #63's residual (`AnthemStatic` color/exclude-source axes). **Still blocked:** redoubled_stormsinger (entered-this-turn copy-set axis wiring, distinct code path from the filter below); brudiclad_telchor_engineer, deekah_fractal_theorist, perplexing_test (token-axis wiring not in this slice).

**2026-07-14:** Added the two missing `PermanentFilter` axes: `entered_this_turn: bool` (backed by a new `Permanent::entered_this_turn` runtime flag, set `true` in `fresh_permanent`/`fresh_token` and reset for every battlefield permanent at each Untap step) and specific-color `ColorFilter::{White,Blue,Black,Red,Green}` (read off `Game::colors_of`), both wired into `permanent_matches`. Fully faithful (note deleted): oran_rief_the_vastwood (`{T}: Put a +1/+1 counter on each green creature that entered this turn` is now `put_counters_each` with `filter = { color = "green", entered_this_turn = true }`). Both axes are general ŌĆö reusable by any future card, not just oran_rief.
**2026-07-14:** Added a further `PermanentFilter` axis, `nonbasic: bool` (CR 205.4a's Basic supertype, read via the existing `is_basic_land` ŌĆö not subtype strings), consulted in `permanent_matches` and therefore at target legality (`legal_targets_for`/`legal_targets`), so an illegal basic-land target is excluded from the enumeration rather than merely rejected at resolution. Trimmed to a precise residual: white_orchid_phantom ŌĆö "destroy up to one target *nonbasic* land" now correctly excludes basic lands from its ETB's legal targets (a basic Island is no longer a legal target); residual note left naming only the dropped "controller ramps a basic" rider (a library search targeted at the destroyed land's controller ŌĆö an arbitrary player ŌĆö which the pool has no shape for). This axis is general, not `white_orchid_phantom`-specific.
**2026-07-15:** perplexing_test's "token-axis wiring not in this slice" note above was stale ŌĆö `PermanentFilter.token` was already wired into `Effect::ReturnAllToHand` via `permanent_matches`, just not adopted by the card. Fully faithful (note deleted): perplexing_test ŌĆö re-authored as two `modal` "choose one" modes (`return_all_to_hand { filter = { types = "creature", token = "token" } }` / `{ token = "nontoken" }`) instead of the collapsed all-creatures union. Pure authoring; no engine change.
**Progress (2026-07-15):** added a further `PermanentFilter` axis, `attached_to_creature: Option<bool>` ŌĆö the mirror of `enchanted`, reading the Aura candidate's OWN host (`attached_to(id)` + `is_creature_on_battlefield`) instead of the host's Aura. Consulted in `permanent_matches`. **Landed:** sages_reverie ŌĆö its ETB draw and static +1/+1 now both count `per_permanent { subtypes = ["Aura"], controller = "you", attached_to_creature = true }` instead of every Aura you control, so an Aura on a noncreature no longer counts (CR 303); Sage's Reverie still counts itself once attached to its enchanted creature. Note deleted, fully faithful. **Still blocked:** unchanged from the entries above. General axis, reusable by any future "attached to a creature" filter.

### 71. `condition-extensions` ŌĆö 12 cards, S ŌĆö **LANDED (2026-07)**
New `Condition` arms plus a conditional-effect wrapper ŌĆö an `if{condition}` gate on an individual effect step inside a `Sequence`, evaluated at that step's resolution (a new eval site; the enum itself is the landed v1 #6 one): you-control-N+-lands ("if you control 4+ lands, untap that land" ŌĆö Fabled Passage; Zimone Prodigy's 8+ draw), a-land-entered-this-turn + prime-number-of-lands (Zimone All-Questioning), source-power-7+ (Yavimaya Bloomsage's becomes-prepared), graveyard card-type counts (spell mastery ŌĆö Animist's Awakening; "N+ cards in your graveyard" ŌĆö Lorehold Archivist), `PlayerHandSizeAtMost` (Naktamun), `YouControlNoSubtype` with a token qualifier (Ophiomancer's "no Snakes", Pest Rescuer's "no Pest token"), `CastInstantOrSorceryThisTurn` on activation gates (Hall of Oracles ŌĆö reads the existing tally), "a creature was exiled this way" (Feral Appetite), and X-threshold branches (Kinetic Ooze's "if X Ōēź 5 / Ōēź 10").
*Cards:* animists_awakening, fabled_passage, feral_appetite, hall_of_oracles, kinetic_ooze, lorehold_archivist, naktamun_lorespinner, ophiomancer, pest_rescuer, yavimaya_bloomsage, zimone_all_questioning, zimone_quandrix_prodigy
**Landed:** added `Effect::Conditional { condition, then }` (per-step gate resolved via the existing intervening-if evaluator), `Condition::{CastInstantOrSorceryThisTurn, YouControlNoSubtype}` (backed by a new turn-scoped `Player::instant_or_sorcery_cast_this_turn` flag and a subtype scan), and `Effect::UntapSearchedLand`. Fully faithful (note deleted): zimone_quandrix_prodigy (8+-land second draw), hall_of_oracles (counter gated on an instant/sorcery cast this turn), ophiomancer ("no Snakes" gate + Snake token). Trimmed: fabled_passage (untap rider now faithful; residual is the fetch-only no-mana flattening), pest_rescuer ("no Pest" gate faithful; residual is the dies-lifegain + lifegain-plus-1 #64/#128).
**Still blocked:** animists_awakening (#65), feral_appetite (#116), kinetic_ooze (#99), lorehold_archivist (#77 prepare/DFC ŌĆö its own back face still needs an upkeep-count-graveyard condition), zimone_all_questioning (prime-count + named-token exotic). naktamun_lorespinner's prepare/DFC blocker cleared ŌĆö see the wheel-effect exotic below. yavimaya_bloomsage's own #77 blocker has since cleared (its Channel back face landed) ŌĆö fully faithful now.

### 72. `self-target-spec` ŌĆö 8 cards, S ŌĆö **LANDED (2026-07)**
A "this permanent, no target" effect address generalizing the landed `PumpSelfUntilEndOfTurn`: `put_counters`, `double_counters`, keyword-grant-until-EOT, and `exile` resolving against the ability's own source (or its attached host ŌĆö Redemption Arc's "exile enchanted creature") instead of any creature you control. Kills the "targets a creature you control but means itself" family of residual notes (Gorma, Hangarback's pump, Forgotten Ancient's counter, Yahenni's counter + indestructible, Primordial Hydra's self-doubling, Leonin Vanguard's self-pump ŌĆö v1 #61's named follow-up).
*Cards:* forgotten_ancient, gorma_the_gullet, hangarback_walker, leonin_vanguard, merchant_of_venom, primordial_hydra, redemption_arc, yahenni_undying_partisan
**Landed:** two non-targeted `TargetSpec` variants ŌĆö `ThisPermanent` ("this") and `EnchantedCreature` ("enchanted_creature") ŌĆö resolve to a fixed reference (the ability's own source, or its attachment host) with no `PendingChoice` and no shroud/hexproof/protection check (CR: these abilities never say "target"). `legal_targets_for` grew a `source: ObjectId` parameter so the two new arms know what "this" means; `place_targeted_ability` (triggers) and `activate_ability` (activated abilities) both short-circuit straight to the stack for these specs instead of pausing. Fully faithful (note deleted): gorma_the_gullet's counter clause, hangarback_walker's pump clause (residual note trimmed to the `{X}{X}`/Thopter-swarm gaps only), primordial_hydra's doubling clause (residual note trimmed to the trample-threshold gap only), yahenni_undying_partisan's counter + indestructible clauses (residual note trimmed to the death-trigger opponent-scoping gap owned by #81), redemption_arc (both abilities faithful, note deleted), leonin_vanguard (self-pump half authored via the landed `PumpSelfUntilEndOfTurn` in a `Sequence`, note deleted). **2026-07-14:** merchant_of_venom's residual sacrifice-watch clause now faithful (authored on the pre-existing `any_player_sacrifices` trigger ŌĆö the note was stale, no new engine surface needed), note deleted. **2026-07-15:** forgotten_ancient's counter clause is now faithful too (authored on the pre-existing `cast_spell`/`any_player` trigger, #93 ŌĆö no new engine surface needed), note trimmed to the move-counters distribution residual only (see #93).

### 73. `multi-target-adoption` ŌĆö 11 cards, M ŌĆö **PARTIALLY LANDED (2026-07)**
Spread v1 #31's landed `TargetCount{min,max}` surface beyond `return_to_hand`: `deal_damage` (with division across up-to-N targets ŌĆö Magma Opus's "4 damage divided as you choose"), `destroy`/`exile`, `tap` (two target permanents), put-counters distribution (one each across up to X ŌĆö Silkguard), X-scaled counts ("destroy up to X" ŌĆö Immoral Bargain; dep #68), "any number of target players", per-extra-target costs (Strive ŌĆö Twinflame), and per-mode target lists inside modal spells (Prismari Charm mode 1's "one or two targets" ŌĆö pairs with #110). The `TargetList` plumbing exists; this is adoption plus the division/count wrinkles.
*Cards:* immoral_bargain, magma_opus, pest_infestation, priest_of_forgotten_gods, prismari_charm, silkguard, striding_shotcaller, twinflame, volcanic_salvo, witch_of_the_moors, zimones_hypothesis

**Landed:** `count: TargetCount` on `deal_damage` and `tap_target` (mirroring `return_to_hand`'s field); `targets: TargetCount` on `put_counters` (named apart from its existing `count: Amount` ŌĆö counters-per-target); a `divided: bool` on `deal_damage` for CR 601.2d division, settled by a new `Game::maybe_begin_damage_division` right after cast-time targets are chosen and answered by a new `PendingChoice::DivideSpellDamage` (reuses `Intent::AssignDamage`'s wire shape and `DamageAssignment`'s division-bookkeeping type ŌĆö branched in `Game::submit` the same way `PayOptionalCost`/`PayOrCounter` already share one intent). Fully faithful (note deleted): volcanic_salvo ("up to two target creatures and/or planeswalkers", `count = {0,2}`, `creature_or_planeswalker` filter ŌĆö only the unrelated power-count cost reduction, #85, stays a residual). Trimmed to a precise residual: magma_opus (damage-division clause is faithful ŌĆö `count = {0,4}`, `divided = true`, deals 4 divided as chosen; the "tap two target permanents" clause stays dropped because the engine resolves only *one* multi-target clause per spell today ŌĆö `Spell.targets` is a single shared list ŌĆö and this card would need two independent ones at once; the tap machinery itself is landed and proven on a standalone test card). silkguard's distribution mechanism is landed and proven standalone too, but the card itself still can't use it ŌĆö its target count is `X`, and `TargetCount` is a fixed range, not tied to `Amount::X` (that gap is #68, not this one's).
**Deferred (named, not attempted):** prismari_charm (per-mode target lists inside a modal spell ŌĆö pairs with #110, a different shape than a single ability's `TargetCount`); immoral_bargain, pest_infestation (X-scaled target counts, same #68 gap as silkguard); twinflame (Strive's escalating per-extra-target cost, #85 additional-cost); priest_of_forgotten_gods ("any number of target players" is an untargeted edict today, `EachPlayerSacrifices{scope}` ŌĆö not cheap, needs a new targeted multi-player edict shape, and its ability is activated, not a spell, so the spell-only multi-target pipeline this wave adopted doesn't reach it anyway); witch_of_the_moors ("up to one" doesn't fall out for free ŌĆö its return effect is a *triggered* ability, and the cast-time `TargetCount`/`ChooseSpellTargets` machinery this wave adopted is `Timing::Spell`-only; a triggered ability's target still goes through the single-target `ChooseTarget` path, which never reads a count ŌĆö same reason Killian, Decisive Mentor's own "tap up to one target creature" ETB trigger stays mandatory). striding_shotcaller and zimones_hypothesis were named in the backlog's card list but aren't real multi-target-adoption candidates: Shotcaller's "put a +1/+1 counter on each of up to X target creatures" text lives entirely on its unmodeled Prepared back face (dropped for an unrelated prereq ŌĆö DFC/Prepared support); Zimone's Hypothesis's own "counter on a creature" primer is a single optional pre-choice, not a targeted multi-target effect.
**Progress (2026-07-11):** closed two of the still-blocked cards, each via a different already-landed prereq. **Fully faithful (note deleted):** witch_of_the_moors ŌĆö re-authored as ONE `end_step` trigger (`[[abilities.effects]]` = `each_player_sacrifices` then `may_return_from_graveyard`), the exact Deadly Brew shape #109 landed; no engine change, the split-trigger and mandatory-return residuals both disappear. prismari_charm ŌĆö mode 1 ("deals 1 damage to each of one or two targets") is now `deal_damage { count = { min = 1, max = 2 } }` inside its mode, genuinely multi-target. This needed one small engine advance: `Game::validate_modes` no longer runs the single-target `targets_are_legal` check against a mode whose own effect is multi-target (it requires `target == None` there instead, deferring to post-cast selection like a non-modal multi-target spell); a new `Game::modal_multi_target` (mirrors `spell_multi_target`, scoped to the *chosen* mode(s)) feeds the existing `choose_spell_targets`/`ChooseSpellTargets` pause; and the modal resolution step-builder in `effects.rs` now expands a multi-target mode's steps from `spell.targets` the same way the non-modal branch already did, instead of using the mode's own (now-`None`) per-mode target slot. Modes 0 and 2 are untouched by this ŌĆö regression-tested that they don't get dragged into multi-target selection. **Still blocked, unchanged:** twinflame (Strive #85), immoral_bargain (sac-driven-X #68/#92), priest_of_forgotten_gods (multi-player targeted edict shape), striding_shotcaller (DFC/Prepared back face). Do NOT mark #73 LANDED ŌĆö four cards remain, each behind a different unlanded prereq.
**Progress (2026-07-12):** closed immoral_bargain. **Fully faithful (note deleted):** immoral_bargain ŌĆö a new `TargetCount.sacrifice_scaled` (the sibling of `x_scaled`, TOML `count = { sacrifice_scaled = true }`), read by `Game::choose_spell_targets` alongside the already-landed `AdditionalCost.sacrifice` (#92) and `Game::spell_sacrifice_count`: X is settled pre-stack by the paid "sacrifice X creatures" additional cost (CR 601.2b/f), then substituted as an always-exact `{X, X}` target count for "destroy X target nonland permanents" (`target = { permanent = { types = "nonland" } }`) ŌĆö no declinable "up to X" case, unlike `x_scaled`. **Still blocked, unchanged:** twinflame (Strive #85), priest_of_forgotten_gods (multi-player targeted edict shape), striding_shotcaller (DFC/Prepared back face). Do NOT mark #73 LANDED ŌĆö three cards remain, each behind a different unlanded prereq.
**Progress (2026-07-12):** closed priest_of_forgotten_gods, landing the "any number of target players" edict shape. New `EdictScope::TargetedPlayers` (TOML `scope = "targeted_players"`) on `EachPlayerSacrifices`: when the edict resolves under this scope, `Game::begin_sacrifice_edict` pauses the controller on a new `PendingChoice::ChooseTargetPlayers` (CR 601.2c/608.2b ŌĆö every living player legal, zero a legal choice, the controller may include themselves) instead of computing an `AllPlayers`/`EachOpponent` scope-derived set; a new `Intent::ChooseTargetPlayers` answers it (`Game::choose_target_players`), applies the chosen players' life loss, and hands off to the same `Game::prompt_next_sacrifice` fan-out the other two scopes already share ŌĆö no change to that per-player sacrifice loop itself. **Fully faithful (note deleted):** priest_of_forgotten_gods ŌĆö the edict now targets exactly the caster's chosen subset (proven not-each-opponent by a 4-player test where an unchosen opponent is left untouched), zero-target and self-target are both covered. **Still blocked, unchanged:** twinflame (Strive #85), striding_shotcaller (DFC/Prepared back face). Do NOT mark #73 LANDED ŌĆö two cards remain, each behind a different unlanded prereq.
**Progress (2026-07-15):** landed `put_counters.divided` ŌĆö the counter twin of `deal_damage.divided` this entry's landed note flagged as a follow-up gap. `Effect::PutCounters` grew `divided: bool` (default `false`): when set, `count` is a total split across the chosen `targets` instead of a per-target amount, mirroring `deal_damage.divided`'s shape exactly ŌĆö a new `Game::maybe_begin_counter_division` (called from the same two sites as `maybe_begin_damage_division`) pauses on a new `PendingChoice::DivideCounters` (reusing `Intent::AssignDamage`'s wire shape and `DamageAssignment`'s bookkeeping type, branched in `Game::submit` alongside `DivideSpellDamage`/`AssignCombatDamage`) once more than one target is chosen; a single chosen target auto-takes the whole total. The split is recorded on a new `Spell::counter_division` field and read back at resolution by the existing `PutCounters` execute arm, through the same replaceable-counters-placement pipeline (CR 614) a non-divided `put_counters` already uses. This isn't one of #73's own 11 listed cards ŌĆö it closes elusive_otter's adventure half (Grove's Bounty), which carried its own standalone `approximates` note pointing at this exact gap ("cf. deal_damage.divided, #73/#96"). **Fully faithful (note deleted):** elusive_otter ŌĆö Grove's Bounty ("Distribute X +1/+1 counters among any number of target creatures you control") is now `count = "x"`, `targets = { min = 0, x_scaled = true }`, `divided = true`. **Follow-up noted, not built:** forgotten_ancient's dropped "move any number of +1/+1 counters distributed as you choose among any number of target creatures" is a *move*-counters distribution (`MoveCounters`), not a *put*-counters one ŌĆö a structurally similar but distinct effect; this rider's `DivideCounters`/`counter_division` plumbing doesn't cover it as-is.
**Progress (2026-07-15, rider):** closed forgotten_ancient's flagged follow-up above. `Effect::MoveCounters` grew `distributed: bool` (default `false`): unlike `put_counters.divided`'s fixed spell-total shape (which needs `Spell::counter_division` bookkeeping a triggered ability's stack item doesn't have), a move's total isn't fixed and isn't spell-scoped, so this pauses on a new `PendingChoice::DivideMovedCounters { from, legal, cap }` ŌĆö `cap` is `from`'s *live* +1/+1 count (a move can't exceed what's actually there), and the answered map may be a proper subset of `legal` summing to anywhere from zero up to `cap` (not required to move them all or use every offered destination), unlike `DivideCounters`'s exact-total/every-target-covered validation. Reuses `Intent::AssignDamage`'s wire shape (routed in `Game::submit` alongside the other three divide-choices) and projects onto the existing `PendingChoiceView::DivideCounters` wire shape unchanged (`crates/schema/src/projection/choice.rs`) ŌĆö no new schema surface, since the client-visible shape ("distribute up to N among these targets") is identical; only the engine-side `PendingChoice` variant differs, so the answer still routes to the right handler. The answer applies the move directly (one combined removal from `from`, then each destination's placement through the existing +1/+1 replacement pipeline) rather than deferring onto continued spell resolution. **Fully faithful (note deleted):** forgotten_ancient ŌĆö the upkeep move now lets the controller move a chosen number (0..=available) of its +1/+1 counters distributed across any number of other target creatures.
**Progress (2026-07-15, rider):** closed zimones_hypothesis ŌĆö the "may put a +1/+1 counter on a creature" primer is now authored as an up-to-one `put_counters` (`targets = { min = 0, max = 1 }`, `target = "creature"`) effect[0] on each odd/even mode ability, placed before the mass bounce reads power; pure authoring plus a small modal/spell resolution-step tweak. `Game::resolve_spell`'s per-ability step expansion dropped a *whole* multi-target ability outright when its declinable (`min = 0`) target was declined (0 chosen) ŌĆö correct for a bare multi-target effect, but wrong once a `Sequence` pairs that declinable step with a target-independent one (the mass bounce), which should still run. Fixed with a new `multi_target_steps` helper (both the modal and non-modal branches) that, on zero chosen targets, pushes one `None`-target step instead of none when `Effect::has_target_independent_step` says some step doesn't need it ŌĆö reusing the same predicate already gating this exact "declined optional target, target-independent step still runs" rule for triggered single-target abilities (Kinetic Ooze); `run()`'s own per-step guard already no-ops the declined counter step while letting the bounce execute. Regression-covered (`zimones_hypothesis_primer_declined`, plus the two pre-existing odd/even tests updated to explicitly decline the now-legal primer choice) and the whole suite stays green, so Silkguard's own identical latent gap (hexproof rider dropped alongside a fully-declined counter distribution) is fixed for free too, though untested here (out of scope). **Still blocked:** twinflame (Strive #85), striding_shotcaller (DFC). Do NOT mark #73 LANDED.
**Progress (2026-07-15, rider):** closed primal_might ŌĆö pump-then-fight now share one cast target (pump targets the ally, the enemy is a resolution-time up-to-one pick, mirroring Effect::Fight's own resolution-time second creature); `Fight { ally_is_shared_target }` the reusable primitive. Not one of #73's own 11 cards (it carried a standalone approximates note). Still blocked: twinflame (Strive #85), striding_shotcaller (DFC).
**Progress (2026-07-15):** closed twinflame, landing Strive (CR 601.2f/702.42) as a new per-extra-target additional cost. `AdditionalCost.strive: Option<&'static Cost>` (TOML `[cost.additional.strive]`, the `[cost]`-shaped sibling of `kicker`). The ordering crux (CR 601.2c chooses targets before CR 601.2f locks the cost, but this engine puts a spell on the stack before pausing to choose multi-targets) is solved the same way immoral_bargain's `sacrifice_scaled` solved it: the caster declares the target count up front ŌĆö a new `Intent::Cast.strive_count: u8` (mirrors `kicked`/`sacrifice_cost`'s cast-time slot) ŌĆö `Game::cast_cost` multiplies `strive.{generic,colored,colorless}` by `strive_count.saturating_sub(1)` and folds it in (pip-sum only, same `ponytail:` as kicker's own fold), and a new `TargetCount.strive_scaled` (the `sacrifice_scaled`/`x_scaled` sibling) has `Game::choose_spell_targets` substitute the declared count as an always-exact `{N, N}` clamp via a new `Game::spell_strive_count` (reads a new `Spell::strive_count`, set from the `SpellCast` event, mirroring `spell_sacrifice_count`). `Game::validate_cast` additionally rejects a declared count that exceeds the legal-target count or `MAX_TARGETS` up front (`Reject::IllegalTarget`) ŌĆö Strive has no separate cost-paying vector to derive the count from (unlike sacrifice), so an over-declared count would otherwise overpay for targets `choose_spell_targets` could never fill. Separately, `create_token_copy` adopted multi-target: a new `targets: TargetCount` field (named apart from its existing `count: Amount`, the "how many targets" vs. "copies per target" split `put_counters` already established) drives the ordinary multi-target step-expansion in `effects.rs`'s `resolve_spell` ŌĆö no special-cased resolution loop, the effect just runs once per chosen target like every other multi-target effect. A new `exile_at_next_end_step: bool` (mirrors `create_token`'s own field, distinct from `sacrifice_at_next_end_step` because exile skips dies-triggers) replaces twinflame's old sacrifice-based cleanup with the oracle-correct exile. **Fully faithful (note deleted):** twinflame ŌĆö Strive's escalating cost, "any number of target creatures you control," one haste copy per chosen target, and end-step exile (not sacrifice) are all scripted and tested (a Zulaport Cutthroat copy proves exile via no dies-trigger firing, versus sacrifice which would). Single-target `create_token_copy` (`count = 1`, `targets` defaulted) is behavior-preserving ŌĆö the existing determined_iteration/rionya/rite_of_replication/leitmotif_composer/replication_technique tests are unchanged. **#73's only remaining card is striding_shotcaller** (DFC/Prepared back face ŌĆö a different unlanded prereq, untouched). Do NOT mark #73 LANDED.
**Progress (2026-07-15):** landed **multiple independent target clauses per spell/ability** and closed magma_opus (and kinetic_ooze, #65's residual). One spell/ability may now carry more than one targeting effect, each with its *own* target set. Spell path: a runtime `Spell::targets_second: TargetList` holds a second clause (clause 0 stays `Spell::targets`, `Copy`-preserving ŌĆö no `Vec` on the `Copy` `Spell`); a new `Game::spell_target_clause(def, n)` enumerates the n-th non-single `Timing::Spell` targeting ability, and `choose_spell_targets` now chains clause-by-clause (`Game::advance_spell_target_clauses`) at cast ŌĆö clause 0 chosen, then clause 1, then the CR 601.2d divided-damage/counter split runs once every clause is settled. `PendingChoice::ChooseSpellTargets` and `Event::SpellTargetsChosen` grew a `clause: u8` (the schema wire view drops it ŌĆö engine-internal ordering); `apply.rs` routes clause 0/1 to the two `TargetList`s; the non-modal resolution step-builder pulls each multi-target ability's targets from its own clause. Ability path: rather than thread a per-clause list onto the `Copy` `StackItem::Ability` (single `target`), a second targeting *step* in a triggered ability's `Sequence` chooses its set **at resolution** (ponytail CR 603.3d) via a new no-target-of-its-own effect `double_counters_on_chosen_creatures` (pauses on a new `PendingChoice::DoubleCountersTargets`, mirrors `phase_out`/`Proliferate`'s any-subset choice, reuses `Intent::ChooseSacrifices`). Two clauses max per spell (bump to a `[TargetList; N]` array when a card prints three ŌĆö none does). **Trimmed to a precise residual:** magma_opus ŌĆö the divided-damage clause *and* the "Tap two target permanents" clause now both resolve with independent cast-time targets; only the alternative `{U/R}{U/R}, Discard this card: Create a Treasure` activated-from-hand ability stays dropped (#82, alt costs), plus the standing division-keyed-by-permanent ponytail (a player can't be a divided target ŌĆö no pool card needs it). **Still blocked:** striding_shotcaller (DFC), magma_opus's #82 residual. Do NOT mark #73 LANDED.
**Progress (2026-07-16):** landed magma_opus's divided-damage-to-a-player residual ŌĆö the standing
"division keyed by permanent, so a player can't be a divided target" ponytail the 2026-07-15 note
left (and its #82 alt-cost residual is already closed by the modeled `[hand_ability]`). The divided
`deal_damage` clause's filter widened from `creature_or_planeswalker` to `target = "any"`
(creature-or-player, CR 601.2d's "any number of targets"). A parallel `Copy`

the object-keyed `DamageAssignment`, and a dedicated `Intent::DivideSpellDamage { assignment:
Vec<(Target, i32)> }` (its own `Target`-keyed wire ŌĆö `WireSpellDamage`/`WireIntent::DivideSpellDamage`
ŌĆö split from combat's object-only `AssignDamage`) lets a player be named in the division answer;
