### 74. `delayed-until-next-turn` ŌĆö 11 cards, M ŌĆö **LANDED (2026-07-15)**
Widen v1 #27's landed `ScheduleAtNextUpkeep` into a general delayed-trigger schedule: `fire_at: Step` (next end step ŌĆö "sacrifice/exile it at the beginning of the next end step", the myriad/Twinflame-family cleanup and Gift of Immortality's return), event-fired one-shots ("the next time you cast an instant or sorcery this turn, copy it" ŌĆö Thunderclap Drake, Surge to Victory), a schedule entry referencing specific minted objects (the tokens to exile, not a re-scan), and the exile-play permission expiring at the end of your *next* turn (Atsushi's residual). One schedule structure, three drain sites.
*Cards:* angel_of_indemnity, atsushi_the_blazing_sky, determined_iteration, ghoulish_impetus, gift_of_immortality, manaform_hellkite, muddle_the_ever_changing, redoubled_stormsinger, rionya_fire_dancer, surge_to_victory, thunderclap_drake
**Progress (2026-07):** generalized `ScheduleAtNextUpkeep` into `fire_at: Step` (renamed the drain to `Game::fire_delayed_triggers`, `scheduled: Vec<(controller, source, Step, Effect)>`), so a schedule can fire at the next end step as well as the next upkeep. Two drain sites of the slice built: (1) `CreateTokenCopy { sacrifice_at_next_end_step }` schedules a `SacrificeObject` against each *specific minted token* (not a re-scan) at `Step::End`; (2) Atsushi's exile-play permission extended to expire at the end of your *next* turn via an `extended` flag on `play_from_exile` that shields the entry from this turn's cleanup, then arms (`Event::PlayFromExilePermissionArmed`) at its controller's next untap so it clears at that turn's cleanup. **Faithful (notes deleted):** atsushi_the_blazing_sky (the impulse-play window now lasts through the controller's next turn; only the standard resolution-time mode-choice ponytail remains). **Trimmed:** determined_iteration ŌĆö the delayed sacrifice at the next end step is modeled; residual note is only the dropped "gains haste" rider (no per-token haste grant on a token minted mid-ability, #88). **Still blocked (untouched):** the event-fired "next time you cast an instant/sorcery, copy it" one-shots (muddle_the_ever_changing, redoubled_stormsinger, rionya_fire_dancer, thunderclap_drake, manaform_hellkite), Gift of Immortality's delayed return, and the myriad-family cleanup (angel_of_indemnity, ghoulish_impetus).
**Progress (2026-07-14, via #69):** surge_to_victory cleared ŌĆö its "copy the exiled card on
combat damage" clause turned out to need a *repeatable, controller-scoped* delayed watch
(`Effect::ScheduleThisTurnCombatDamageCopy`/`pending_combat_damage_copy`), not this entry's
event-armed-but-one-shot `pending_next_cast` shape (Thunderclap Drake's "next cast" is a
different CR 603.7 duration than "whenever ... this turn"). Landed under #69, not this entry;
still counts against this entry's card list as done. The remaining event-fired "next cast, copy
it" one-shots (thunderclap_drake et al.) are unaffected and still blocked.
**Progress (2026-07-11):** landed the event-armed sibling of `scheduled` this entry's sketch called for ŌĆö a *third* drain site, event-fired rather than step-fired. `Effect::ScheduleNextCastTrigger { filter, then }` arms a `pending_next_cast: Vec<(controller, source, SpellFilter, &'static [Effect])>` queue (`Event::NextCastTriggerArmed`); a new `Game::fire_next_cast_triggers` (its own `PostIntentPhase::NextCastTriggers`, right after `DelayedTriggers`) scans each batch's `Event::SpellCast` and fires+removes (`Event::NextCastTriggerConsumed`, CR 603.7's "next" ŌĆö at most once) every armed watch whose controller cast a spell matching its filter, contextualizing `then` with the triggering spell's `{X}` exactly like `queue_cast_spell_triggers` already does; an unconsumed watch is cleared at the next turn's Untap (same boundary `spells_cast_this_turn` resets at). Also widened `Effect::is_mana_ability` to recognize a `Sequence` containing an `AddMana` step (CR 605.3a doesn't require a mana ability to do *only* that) and switched the mana-ability resolution path (cast.rs) from a bare `execute_effect` call to `resolve_effect`, so a composite mana ability resolves every step off-stack instead of panicking on `Sequence`. **This landed exactly one card, and it's a #68 card, not one of this entry's own** ŌĆö brass_infiniscope (see #68's note below); none of #74's own 11 listed cards are touched yet. **Still blocked, unchanged:** the event-fired "copy the triggering spell" one-shots (muddle_the_ever_changing, redoubled_stormsinger, rionya_fire_dancer, surge_to_victory, thunderclap_drake, manaform_hellkite ŌĆö the new queue's *shape* fits, but each needs a command-zone-cast counter and/or copy-the-triggering-spell machinery this wave didn't build), Gift of Immortality's delayed return, and the myriad-family cleanup. Do NOT mark #74 LANDED.
**Progress (2026-07-12):** built the copy-the-triggering-spell primitive this entry's "copy" drain site was still missing. `TriggerContext` grew `triggering_spell: Option<ObjectId>`, set from the matched `Event::SpellCast { spell, .. }` in `fire_next_cast_triggers` alongside the existing `cast_x`, and baked into a placed trigger's effect tree by a new `fill_triggering_spell` walker (mirrors `fill_dying_enchanted_creature`). New `Effect::CopyTriggeringSpell { triggering_spell, count, may_choose_new_targets }` resolves by reusing `mint_spell_copies`' existing mint-plus-retarget path (`may_choose_new_targets = true`, every current consumer) or a bare mint with no retarget (`false`, CR 707.10c's declined case ŌĆö not exercised by any pool card yet); guard-returns with no copies if `triggering_spell` is `None` or has already left the stack (countered in response, CR 603.4). **Faithful (note deleted):** thunderclap_drake ŌĆö all three abilities now scripted: the static reducer's `filter` switched from the `noncreature` stand-in to the real `SpellFilter::InstantOrSorcery` (the arm already existed, unused by this card until now), and the `{2}{U}, Sacrifice this creature` ability is `schedule_next_cast_trigger { filter = "instant_or_sorcery", then = [{ type = "copy_triggering_spell", count = "commander_casts_from_command_zone", may_choose_new_targets = true }] }`. **Still blocked:** muddle_the_ever_changing and redoubled_stormsinger (need myriad/become-a-copy machinery, not this primitive), rionya_fire_dancer (needs begin-combat-cast tracking + #89), surge_to_victory (copies a spell from a *graveyard*, not the stack ŌĆö a distinct source, not this primitive), manaform_hellkite (its cast trigger creates a token, not a spell copy ŌĆö this entry's card list mis-scoped it; already scripted via #89's `create_token`/`set_base_pt`, unrelated to this primitive, with a residual #101 mana-spent-to-cast gap). Do NOT mark #74 LANDED ŌĆö angel_of_indemnity, ghoulish_impetus (myriad-family cleanup) and gift_of_immortality (delayed return) are also still untouched.
**Progress (2026-07-12):** landed Gift of Immortality's delayed return, the last item this entry's original sketch named ("Gift of Immortality's return"). This entry landed piecemeal across #69/#79/#88/#89/#101/#127/#130 rather than as one build, matching its "one schedule structure, three drain sites" sketch.

### 75. `counter-kinds` ŌĆö 6 cards, M ŌĆö **LANDED (2026-07)**
The kind-keyed counter map v1 #39 deliberately deferred (only the finality bool landed): charge/story/vow/study counters as a small `(kind ŌåÆ count)` map on `Permanent`, with enters-with-N-of-kind, accrual triggers, remove-N-of-kind as an activation cost (Staff of the Storyteller's "{W}, remove a story counter: draw"), counter-count conditions, and counter-scaled `AddMana` ("add one mana per charge counter" ŌĆö Astral Cornucopia, Elementalist's Palette). The `+1/+1` path and its replacement pipeline stay untouched; the map is for named non-P/T kinds.
*Cards:* astral_cornucopia, elementalists_palette, lattice_library, mana_bloom, promise_of_loyalty, staff_of_the_storyteller

**Landed:** a `CounterKind` enum (`Charge`, `Story` ŌĆö only the kinds real cards land) keying a fixed `Permanent::kind_counters: [u8; 2]` array (kept off the +1/+1 replacement pipeline); `Effect::EntersWithCounters` grew `kind: Option<CounterKind>` (`None` = the +1/+1 path, `Some(k)` places the raw amount in the kind map), `ActivationCost::remove_counters_kind` (remove-N-of-kind as a cost, gated by CR 602.2b), `Amount::PerCounterOfKindOnSource`, `Condition::SourceHasNoCountersOfKind` (the "== 0" intervening-if), and `Event::KindCountersPlaced` (+ its `VisibleEvent` mirror ŌĆö counters are public). Fully faithful (note deleted): mana_bloom (enters with X charge counters, "remove a charge counter: add one mana of any color" once-each-turn, upkeep self-bounce when it has no charge counters ŌĆö its whole cost is a single `{X}`, so #68's multiplier gap never applies). Trimmed to a precise residual: astral_cornucopia (enters-with-X-charge + `{T}: one mana per charge counter` now faithful; the `{X}{X}{X}` cost stays a single `{X}` ŌĆö `Cost.x` is a bool not a u8 multiplier, #68), staff_of_the_storyteller (the `{W}, {T}, remove a story counter: draw` ability now faithful; the story-counter *accrual* trigger stays dropped, blocked on #81's `Trigger::YouCreateToken`), promise_of_loyalty (the vow counter's "can't attack you / your planeswalkers" restriction stays dropped ŌĆö per-creature attack restrictions aren't wired into declare-attackers legality, #80 ŌĆö and the counter itself is left unplaced since it has no observable effect without that restriction).
**Progress (2026-07-11):** added `SpendRestriction::HasX` ("spend this mana only on costs that contain `{X}`", CR 106.9) ŌĆö the one primitive the note's "restricted + counter-scaled `AddMana` wiring" gap was actually missing, since restricted mana (#120) and counter-scaled `AddMana` (`repeat = { per_counter_of_kind = "charge" }`, this entry's own `astral_cornucopia` half) had both already landed separately. **Fully faithful (note deleted):** elementalists_palette ŌĆö all three abilities now scripted, including the `{T}: Add {C} for each charge counter... Spend this mana only on costs that contain {X}` tap (`add_mana`, `mana = ["colorless"]`, `repeat = { per_counter_of_kind = "charge" }`, `restriction = "has_x"`).
**Progress (2026-07-11):** added `CounterKind::Study` (`COUNT` 2 ŌåÆ 3, `kind_counters: [u8; 3]`) ŌĆö the one primitive lattice_library's note was still missing, since the "first {X} spell each turn" cast trigger (#67/#68) and a token entering with variable +1/+1 counters (#89) had both already landed separately. **Fully faithful (note deleted):** lattice_library ŌĆö `enters_with_counters { count = "x", kind = "study" }` places the study counters as the enchantment enters (its whole cost is a single `{X}`, so #68's multiplier gap never applies), and both the ETB and the recurring `cast_spell { spell_filter = "has_x", nth_each_turn = 1 }` trigger mint a 0/0 Fractal with `enters_with = { per_counter_of_kind = "study" }`, sized live to the study counters already on the enchantment.

### 76. `search-library-extensions` ŌĆö 7 cards, M ŌĆö **LANDED (2026-07, partial pool)**
Search widenings on the landed search flow: wire `CardFilter::LandWithSubtype` (landed for Nature's Lore) into the remaining consumers (Three Visits' Forest, Claim Jumper's Plains), "up to N" in one search with one shuffle + reveal (Land Tax's three basics, Cultivate's two, Springbloom's two ŌĆö a repeat-select loop in the existing search `PendingChoice`), search-to-battlefield-tapped as a destination, and the catch-up "repeat this process once" rider (Claim Jumper). Also the opponent-landfall trigger already landed for Archaeomancer's Map ŌĆö its "put a land from hand" search half rides here.
*Cards:* archaeomancers_map, bitterthorn_nissas_animus, claim_jumper, cultivate, land_tax, springbloom_druid, three_visits

**Landed:** `Effect::SearchLibrary` grew a `count: u8` (default 1, `de::one_u8`) ŌĆö the max cards one search may find; `PendingChoice::SearchLibrary` grew `remaining: u8` and `search_library` now re-pauses (over `matches` minus the pick) after a found card while `remaining > 1` and matches are left, shuffling only once at the true end (CR 701.19f) ŌĆö a fail-to-find still ends the search immediately, always legal. Fully faithful (notes deleted): three_visits (`land_with_subtype = ["Forest"]`, matching Nature's Lore's spelling), land_tax (`count = 3`). Trimmed to a precise residual: springbloom_druid (`count = 2` now faithful; the "sacrifice a land" additional-cost gate stays dropped ŌĆö no ETB-trigger additional cost in the DSL), archaeomancers_map (`count = 2` + `land_with_subtype = ["Plains"]` now faithful; the filter also matches a nonbasic Plains-typed land ŌĆö e.g. a check land ŌĆö which the printed "basic Plains cards" wording excludes, and the pool has several such duals), claim_jumper (a real `[[abilities]]` ETB now exists ŌĆö `count = 2` search for Plains to battlefield tapped, gated on the opponent-lands intervening-if ŌĆö but "repeat this process once" re-checks that condition *between* the two fetches, which `search_library`'s repeat-loop doesn't thread; modeled as a flat `count = 2`, a broadening once the opponent catches up mid-search).
**Left blocked:** bitterthorn_nissas_animus (Living weapon ŌĆö auto-create-and-attach token on ETB ŌĆö has no engine entry point; its attack-trigger land search is otherwise exactly this wave's shape and would be trivial once living weapon lands).
**Progress (2026-07-11):** `Effect::SearchLibrary` grew `overflow: Option<SearchDest>` (default none) ŌĆö the first find still lands on `to_zone`, every find after the first lands on `overflow` instead, carried on `PendingChoice::SearchLibrary` and applied in `search_library`'s re-pause (`dest: overflow.unwrap_or(dest)`), so one search can now route to two destinations while still shuffling once (CR 701.19f). Fully faithful (note deleted): cultivate ŌĆö one `search_library` (`count = 2`, `to_zone = "battlefield"`, `tapped = true`, `overflow = "hand"`) replaces the old two-independent-searches modeling; the "reveal those cards" clause stays unmodeled (searches reveal nothing to opponents in this engine, the same untracked gap Land Tax's "reveal them" already carries with no note).
**Still blocked:** bitterthorn_nissas_animus (unchanged ŌĆö blocked on Living Weapon, an external increment, not this increment's search shape; its attack-trigger land search is otherwise exactly this shape and lands trivially once Living Weapon does).
**Progress (2026-07-15):** bitterthorn_nissas_animus landed via #79 once Living Weapon (`Effect::AttachSelfToMintedToken`, #89) closed the blocker ŌĆö the search half was already exactly this wave's shape (`filter = "basic_land"`, `to_zone = "battlefield"`, `tapped = true`). **Faithful (note deleted):** bitterthorn_nissas_animus.
**Progress (2026-07-15):** closed claim_jumper's "repeat this process once" re-gate residual with no engine change ŌĆö its ETB is now two sequenced `search_library` effects (`count` defaults to 1), the second wrapped in `Effect::Conditional { condition = opponent_controls_more_lands }`, so the second fetch is re-evaluated live at resolution (after the first Plains has entered) and cancels once land parity is reached (the flat `count = 2` broadening in the "Landed" line above is gone). **Faithful (note deleted):** claim_jumper. Tests: `claim_jumper_second_fetch_regated_on_land_parity` (opponent ahead by one ŌåÆ the second search never opens), `claim_jumper_fetches_two_when_still_behind` (ahead by two ŌåÆ it opens and fetches). **Still blocked:** none remaining ŌĆö the full #76 pool is now faithful.

### 77. `prepare-back-face-authoring` ŌĆö 7 cards, M ŌĆö **LANDED (2026-07)**
Author the remaining soc prepare cards onto the *landed* v1 #46 `CardDef::back`/`CastPrepared` machinery ŌĆö each blocked only on small back-face verbs, most of which land in other v2 increments: each-player-loses-life (Vandal's Edit ŌĆö Defacing Duskmage), draw-X + `ManaValueAtLeast` reducer (Braingeyser ŌĆö Dirgur, dep #67/#68), Pest-per-opponent (Turn Stones ŌĆö Eccentric Pestfinder, dep #64), Replenish mass return (Eiganjo, dep #69), Stensian's X-drain + combat-chain triggers, Striding Shotcaller's X-multitarget face (dep #73), Yavimaya Bloomsage's power-7 condition + EOT-mana-grant face (dep #71). This entry is the authoring sweep once those verbs exist.
*Cards:* defacing_duskmage, dirgur_focusmage, eccentric_pestfinder, eiganjo_dynastorian, stensian_sanguinist, striding_shotcaller, yavimaya_bloomsage

**Progress (2026-07-11):** authored the prepare cards whose front trigger and back-face verb were
already landed, onto the existing v1 #46 `[back]`/`CastPrepared` machinery ŌĆö zero engine changes
needed (the stale approximates notes claiming "no prepared/DFC support" were wrong since #46).
**Faithful (notes deleted):** eiganjo_dynastorian (`you_attack_with_creatures at_least = 2` ŌåÆ
`become_prepared`; Replenish back face is `mass_return_from_graveyard { filter = "enchantment" }`,
covered by the new `prepare_eiganjo_replenish_returns_enchantments` test), defacing_duskmage
(`player_draws { drawer = "opponent", nth_each_turn = 2 }` ŌåÆ `become_prepared`; Vandal's Edit back
face composes `draw_cards` + `each_opponent_loses_life` + `lose_life`, ponytail-noted as sequential
rather than CR-simultaneous "each player loses 2 life" ŌĆö unobservable for the pool). **Still
blocked:** dirgur_focusmage (front trigger needs a cast-zone qualifier, "from your hand",
#67/#68), stensian_sanguinist (combat-damage-to-a-player trigger + grant-deathtouch, #65/#97),
striding_shotcaller (X-multitarget back face, #73), yavimaya_bloomsage (target-power condition +
Channel restricted-mana back face, #75/#120). Do not mark #77 LANDED ŌĆö four cards remain, all
blocked.

**Progress (2026-07-11):** landed the token-controller fix eccentric_pestfinder was waiting on ŌĆö
new `TokenController::OnePerOpponent` (mints one token per opponent, all under the ability's own
controller), distinct from the existing `EachOpponent` (one per opponent, each under that
opponent). Turn Stones' back face now wires `create_token controller = "one_per_opponent"`, so
"For each opponent, *you* create a ... Pest ..." routes every minted Pest's "when this dies, you
gain 1 life" to the actual caster instead of the opponent who happened to receive it. **Faithful
(note deleted):** eccentric_pestfinder.

**Progress (2026-07-12):** landed the cast-zone qualifier dirgur_focusmage was waiting on ŌĆö a new
`from_hand: bool` on `Trigger::CastSpell` (`#[serde(default)]` false = the existing "any zone"
behavior), read off a new `Spell::cast_from_hand` engine-internal flag set at `Event::SpellCast`
apply time (`self.zone_of(from) == Zone::Hand`, checked before the source card moves onto the
stack) ŌĆö no `Event`/schema surface, the flag never leaves `Spell`. Along the way, closed a second,
until-now-unnoticed gap the card's own back face needed: `Game::cast_prepared`
hardcoded its cast's `{X}` to 0 (`Intent::CastPrepared` had no `x` field at all), so an `{X}` back
face like Braingeyser could never draw more than zero cards. `Intent::CastPrepared` and
`Event::PreparedSpellCast` both grow an `x: u32` (mirroring `Intent::Cast`'s), threaded through
`cast_prepared`'s cost/target legality the same way `validate_cast` already does ŌĆö a small wire
surface addition (`crates/schema` mirrors), unlike the `from_hand` flag itself. **Faithful (note
deleted):** dirgur_focusmage ŌĆö reducer tightened to `instant_or_sorcery` (was `noncreature`), the
prepare trigger gated on instant-or-sorcery + MVŌēź5 + `from_hand = true`, Braingeyser's back face
drawing `{X}` cards to a target player. **Still blocked, untouched:** stensian_sanguinist
(combat-damage-to-a-player trigger + grant-deathtouch, #65/#97), striding_shotcaller
(X-multitarget back face, #73), yavimaya_bloomsage (target-power condition + Channel
restricted-mana back face, #75/#120). Do not mark #77 LANDED ŌĆö three cards remain, all blocked.

**Progress (2026-07-12):** landed striding_shotcaller ŌĆö its blocker ("X-multitarget back face,
#73") was stale: #68 (`TargetCount.x_scaled`) and #73 (silkguard's `put_counters.targets` shape)
are both landed, so the front trigger (`deals_combat_damage_to_player`/`who = "your_creatures"` ŌåÆ
`become_prepared`) and the back face's per-target counter+flying (one `[[back.abilities]]` whose
`put_counters`/`pump_until_end_of_turn` steps share a `Sequence` target, re-run once per chosen
creature by the existing non-modal multi-target expansion) plus the separate single-fire
`draw_cards` ability were pure authoring, no DSL surface added. One real engine gap surfaced along
the way, not anticipated by the dispatch: `Game::cast_prepared` had never been wired to the
choose-after-cast multi-target flow `Game::cast_with_kind` already gives a directly-cast
multi-target spell (`Intent::CastPrepared` only ever accepted a single up-front `target`, so
casting a prepared *multi*-target back face rejected with `IllegalTarget` before payment). Fixed
at `cast_prepared` itself ŌĆö reuses the existing `spell_multi_target`/`choose_spell_targets`/
`PendingChoice::ChooseSpellTargets` machinery verbatim, no new `Effect`/`Event`/schema surface,
same "up to X"-is-declinable and X=0-forces-empty-choice semantics a direct multi-target cast
already has. **Faithful (note deleted):** striding_shotcaller. **Still blocked, untouched:**
stensian_sanguinist (delayed "that creature deals combat damage" prepared trigger +
grant-deathtouch-to-a-targeted-creature, #65/#97), yavimaya_bloomsage (target-power condition +
Channel restricted-mana back face, #75/#120). Do not mark #77 LANDED ŌĆö two cards remain, both
blocked.

**Progress (2026-07-12):** landed stensian_sanguinist fully, and yavimaya_bloomsage's front face.
Stensian's clause A ("Whenever you attack, target creature gains deathtouch until end of turn")
is pure authoring onto the landed `pump_until_end_of_turn`/`you_attack_with_creatures` primitives.
Clause B ("Whenever that creature deals combat damage to a player this combat, this creature
becomes prepared") was the real gap: a new object-scoped CR 603.7 delayed watch, sibling to #74's
filter-scoped `ScheduleNextCastTrigger`/`pending_next_cast` ŌĆö a new `Effect::ArmCombatDamageWatch`
(no target/filter of its own; reads the enclosing `pump_until_end_of_turn` step's shared target)
arms `Game::pending_combat_damage_watch: Vec<(controller, source, watched)>` via a new
`Event::CombatDamageWatchArmed`; a new `Game::fire_combat_damage_watch_triggers` (its own
`PostIntentPhase::CombatDamageWatchTriggers`, mirroring `fire_next_cast_triggers`) scans
`Event::CombatDamageDealtToPlayer` each batch, fires a placeholder-`Trigger` `BecomePrepared`
ability for any matching `watched` id, and removes the entry via `Event::CombatDamageWatchConsumed`;
an unconsumed watch is cleared at `Step::EndCombat`'s `StepBegan` (CR "this combat" ŌĆö narrower
than `pending_next_cast`'s turn-boundary expiry). The back face, Exsanguinate, needed one more
fix: `Effect::EachOpponentDrain` only ever gained the controller a flat per-opponent `amount`
(correct for Zulaport Cutthroat/Silverquill Charm/Eriette, all fixed-number gains) ŌĆö Exsanguinate's
"you gain life equal to the life lost this way" is the *summed* total across every opponent, a
real divergence in a 3+ player pod. Added `sum_gain: bool` (default `false`, existing cards
unchanged) to gate the summed reading. **Fully faithful (note deleted): stensian_sanguinist** ŌĆö
both front-face clauses and the Exsanguinate back face, covered by five new tests (deathtouch
grant + expiry, the watch firing off the *targeted* creature specifically, a non-targeted
creature's damage not arming it, the watch clearing at end of combat so a later combat's damage
from the same object doesn't stale-fire, and Exsanguinate's summed lifegain in a 3-player pod).
yavimaya_bloomsage's front face needed a new `Condition::TargetPowerAtLeast { at_least }` ŌĆö no
existing `Condition` arm reads the *resolving effect's own chosen target's* power (only
`TriggerContext`-derived reads existed); special-cased directly in the `Effect::Conditional`
resolve site against the shared `target` (mirroring how `ability_condition_holds` special-cases
source-based conditions `TriggerContext` can't reach), with a `false` fallback arm in
`condition_holds` itself for exhaustiveness. The `put_counters` + `conditional { become_prepared }`
two-step `effects` sequence is pure authoring once the condition existed. **yavimaya_bloomsage:
front face faithful, Channel back face still TRIMMED** ŌĆö Channel (an activate-from-hand
mana-ability-window special action with a life payment) has no landed primitive; flag-don't-force,
left unauthored per #75/#120. Do not mark #77 LANDED ŌĆö yavimaya_bloomsage carries a residual.

**Progress (2026-07-14):** landed yavimaya_bloomsage's Channel back face, closing #77's last
residual. The one real gap was a *player*-scoped granted mana ability ŌĆö every existing granted
mana ability (`grant_mana_ability`, Goldspan/Galazeth) attaches to a surviving permanent source,
but Channel is cast from hand and its copy leaves nothing behind to hang a `Game::ability_at`
grant off of. Modeled as a fieldless `Effect::GrantChannelColorlessManaThisTurn` that sets a new
per-turn flag (`Player::channel_colorless_mana_this_turn`, cleared at the next Untap alongside
`flash_permission_this_turn`) via a new `Event::ChannelColorlessManaGranted` (+ its
`VisibleEvent` mirror ŌĆö public, no redaction, mirroring `FlashPermissionGranted`). The granted
"pay 1 life: add {C}" action itself is a new standalone `Intent::ChannelColorlessMana` (mirroring
`Intent::TapForMana`'s directness) rather than a `meaningful_actions`/`ability_at`-enumerated
ability ŌĆö a **ponytail**: CR 602/605's "any time you could activate a mana ability" window isn't
independently gated, the action is just legal whenever the flag holds (like every other mana
ability in this engine), and it isn't wired into the client's `paid_mana_activates` radial (which
already excludes every other pay-life mana ability, permanent or not) ŌĆö a client-surfacing
follow-up, not an engine gap. **Fully faithful (note deleted): yavimaya_bloomsage** ŌĆö front
trigger, `become_prepared`, and the Channel back face (`[back.kind] = instant`, no printed mana
cost, one `grant_channel_colorless_mana_this_turn` effect), covered by a new authoring test (the
back face parses to the grant) and a full front-trigger ŌåÆ prepare ŌåÆ cast-copy ŌåÆ pay-life-for-{C}
ŌåÆ expires-at-Untap test. **#77 is now fully LANDED** ŌĆö all seven cards faithful.

### 78. `sacrifice-cost-filters` ŌĆö 8 cards, S ŌĆö **LANDED (2026-07)**
`SacrificeCost` grows a `PermanentFilter` axis beyond None/This/Creature: "another creature" (`other: true` ŌĆö Izoni's sac outlet can currently eat itself; Umbral Zealot, Wight, Woe Strider, Yahenni), subtype sacs ("sacrifice a Food" ŌĆö Gilded Goose's mana ability, Gyome, Goose Mother), "a creature or artifact". The filter struct and its `matches` already exist ŌĆö this is swapping the closed enum's payload and updating the two sacrifice choke points.
*Cards:* gilded_goose, gyome_master_chef, izoni, the_goose_mother, umbral_collar_zealot, wight_of_the_reliquary, woe_strider, yahenni_undying_partisan
**Landed:** `SacrificeCost::Creature` now carries a `PermanentFilter` (bare-string `"creature"` sugar still parses to an any-creature-you-control filter; `{ creature = { other = true } }` adds "another creature" self-exclusion), consulted at both choke points (`activate_ability`'s cost resolution and `sacrifice_candidates`). Fully faithful (note deleted): izoni's sac-outlet clause (residual note trimmed to the Insect token's color only, #63/#64), wight_of_the_reliquary's sac-outlet clause (residual note trimmed to the dynamic P/T only, #95), woe_strider's sac-outlet clause (residual note trimmed to the Goat token's color only, #64), yahenni_undying_partisan's sac-outlet clause (residual note trimmed to the death-trigger/self-target clauses owned by #72). Trimmed to a precise residual: umbral_collar_zealot ("or artifact" sacrifice option still dropped ŌĆö no artifact-sac filter target in the pool).
**Progress (2026-07-12):** landed the "Sacrifice a Food" residual named above, as part of #65's Food-sacrifice-family slice ŌĆö `SacrificeCost::Creature`'s two choke points (`activate_ability`, `sacrifice_candidates`) now accept *any* permanent matching the filter, not just a creature (the variant keeps its name; a `// ponytail:` on it notes the widened scope), and `de.rs` grows a `{ permanent = { ŌĆ” } }` sacrifice-cost table key that leaves `types` unforced (the existing `{ creature = { ŌĆ” } }` key is unchanged, still forcing `types = creature`). Fully faithful (notes deleted): gilded_goose (its "{T}, Sacrifice a Food: Add one mana of any color" ŌĆö the last residual off #78's own Food-mint slice), gyome_master_chef (needed both this and #65's `nontoken_creatures_entered_this_turn` amount ŌĆö see #65), the_goose_mother (pure authoring once Food-sacrifice and `may_sacrifice`'s existing subtype-filter axis covered it ŌĆö no engine change of its own), umbral_collar_zealot ("Sacrifice another creature or artifact" is now `sacrifice = { permanent = { types = "artifact_or_creature", other = true } }` ŌĆö the `{ permanent = { ŌĆ” } }` key's unforced `types` plus the existing `artifact_or_creature` type-union filter value cover it, pure authoring, no engine change). **Not still blocked** ŌĆö #78 is now fully landed; nothing on its card list remains open.

## Tier 2 ŌĆö multi-card M/L increments

### 79. `attach-riders` ŌĆö 7 cards, M ŌĆö **LANDED (2026-07, partial pool)**
Attach an Aura/Equipment as part of effect resolution: "if it's an Aura, you may attach it to the token" (Ajani's Chosen), Animate Dead attaching itself to the reanimated creature, "attached to that token" (Forum Filibuster), Fractal Harness's ETB self-attach, and move/re-attach with a choose-host `PendingChoice` ("when a creature enters, you may attach this to it" ŌĆö Screams from Within; "return this from your graveyard attached to a new creature" ŌĆö Shielded by Faith). Sketch: an `attach_to{target|minted-token|reanimated|chosen-host}` effect step reusing the existing attachment state, sequenced after the create/reanimate step; the choose-host form adds one `PendingChoice`.
*Cards:* ajanis_chosen, animate_dead, bitterthorn_nissas_animus, forum_filibuster, fractal_harness, screams_from_within, shielded_by_faith
**Landed:** three fieldless read-back attach steps sequenced after the create/reanimate step, reusing the existing `Event::AttachedTo` state ŌĆö `Effect::AttachTriggeringAuraToMintedToken` (reads the just-minted token off this resolution's own `Event::TokenCreated`, attaches the triggering Aura if it is one ŌĆö Ajani's Chosen), `Effect::AttachSelfToEntering` (attaches the ability's own source to the `permanent_enters` permanent; the "may" is the ability's `optional` flag / existing `MayYesNo` surface ŌĆö Shielded by Faith), and `Effect::AttachSelfToReanimated` (reads the just-reanimated permanent off this resolution's own `Event::ReanimatedToBattlefield` ŌĆö Animate Dead). `contextualize_effect`/`fill_entering_permanent` now recurse into a `Sequence` so a create-then-attach ability shares the one entering id. Bug fixed with regression coverage: `Event::AttachedTo`'s characteristics-cache invalidation only dropped the new host, never the vacated old host (a creature that lost an Aura's grant kept stale cached P/T/keywords). **Faithful (notes deleted):** ajanis_chosen, shielded_by_faith. **Trimmed:** animate_dead ŌĆö now reanimates and attaches the Aura to the reanimated creature; residual note is only the -1/-0 penalty (#126) and "sacrifice it when this Aura leaves the battlefield" (#87).
**Still blocked:** forum_filibuster, screams_from_within (choose-host `PendingChoice` move/re-attach ŌĆö untouched). fractal_harness's ETB self-attach landed via #89 (2026-07-12) as the analogous `Effect::AttachSelfToMintedToken` ŌĆö no longer blocked.
**Progress (2026-07-13):** the *deploy-time* choose-host form landed ŌĆö `PendingChoice::ChooseAttachHostForAura` / `Intent::ChooseAttachHost` / `Game::choose_attach_host`, raised by `Game::maybe_pause_attach_deployed_aura` whenever an Aura is put onto the battlefield without being cast (Songbirds' Blessing #84, Armored Skyhunter #94), reusing the Aura spell's own `enchant`-restriction target legality; with no legal host it stays unattached for CR 704.5m to sweep. This is a sibling to ŌĆö not ŌĆö the *move/re-attach* form still owed forum_filibuster and screams_from_within (return-from-graveyard-attached / when-a-creature-enters), which stay blocked.
**Progress (2026-07-13, later same day):** screams_from_within landed, reusing the just-built `ChooseAttachHostForAura` deploy-time pause directly (`Game::begin_return_aura_from_graveyard_attached_to_chosen_host` moves the Aura graveyardŌåÆbattlefield unattached, then calls `Game::maybe_pause_attach_deployed_aura` verbatim ŌĆö see #74/#87's 2026-07-13 notes for the full mechanism). **Faithful (note deleted):** screams_from_within. **Still blocked:** forum_filibuster ("attached to that token" ŌĆö a different read-back address, not a choose-host pause).
**Progress (2026-07-15):** bitterthorn_nissas_animus landed ŌĆö pure card authoring, no engine change. Living Weapon composes the already-landed `Effect::AttachSelfToMintedToken` (#89) as an ETB `create_token` ŌåÆ `attach_self_to_minted_token` pair (the token enters 0/0 but the Equipment's own `grant_to_attached` +1/+1 lands the same resolution, so it survives as a 1/1, mirroring fractal_harness); the attack-trigger land search composes `Effect::SearchLibrary { filter = "basic_land", to_zone = "battlefield", tapped = true }` (#76) with `optional = true` and `timing = "equipped_creature_attacks"` (#89's `EnchantedCreatureAttacks` alias). **Faithful (note deleted):** bitterthorn_nissas_animus.

### 80. `attack-restriction-statics` ŌĆö 7 cards, L ŌĆö **LANDED (2026-07-15)**
The unlanded restriction half of v1 #52: "can't block" (Bloodghast), "can block only creatures with flying" (Brazen Borrower), "Inklings can't attack you" (Combat Calligrapher), "enchanted creatures can't attack you or a planeswalker you control" (Eriette), "attacks each combat if able" (Furygale's tokens), per-creature vow-marked "can't attack you" (Promise of Loyalty, dep #75), plus the attack tax's flat amount becoming an `Amount` evaluated per attacker (Nils' "pay {X} where X is the number of counters on it" ŌĆö rides the landed v1 #52 tax slice). Sketch: restriction/requirement statics fed into the existing declare-attackers/blockers legality checks in `combat.rs`, filter-scoped per defender.
*Cards:* bloodghast, brazen_borrower, combat_calligrapher, eriette_of_the_charmed_apple, furygale_flocking, nils_discipline_enforcer, promise_of_loyalty

**Progress (2026-07-11):** landed the block-restriction half and the "can't attack you" attack-restriction half. Two new block-legality keyword tags on the shared `Game::can_block` check: `cant_block` (CR 509.1a, Bloodghast) and `can_block_only_flyers` (Brazen Borrower's printed static ŌĆö not a named MTG keyword, a card-specific tag like `lesser_power_cant_block`). New `Effect::CantBeAttackedBy { filter }` ŌĆö a `timing = "static"` attack restriction scanned per declared (attacker, defender) pair in `Game::declare_attackers`, mirroring `attack_tax_owed`'s defender-permanent enumeration, `filter`-scoped so only the static's own controller is protected; plus a new `enchanted_by_you` `PermanentFilter` axis ("enchanted by an Aura you control", reusing `auras_controlled_by_attached_to`). ponytail-noted: the "or planeswalkers you control" clause is unobservable while every attack target is a `PlayerId` (planeswalker defenders unmodeled ŌĆö same as Mangara/Tomik in #91). **Fully faithful (note deleted):** eriette_of_the_charmed_apple (its end-step drain was already scripted). **Trimmed:** bloodghast (residual: conditional haste + landfall self-reanimation), brazen_borrower (residual: the Petty Theft adventure half, #131), combat_calligrapher (residual: the tapped-and-attacking token trigger, #88). **Still blocked:** furygale_flocking (forced-attack *requirement* scoped to minted tokens this turn ŌĆö a whole requirement pipeline), nils_discipline_enforcer (counter-scaled attack *tax* + per-player multi-target ŌĆö #68 X-in-costs + #102), promise_of_loyalty (vow-counter-marked "can't attack you" ŌĆö needs a Vow `CounterKind`, #75 landed only Charge/Story). Do not mark #80 LANDED.

**Progress (2026-07-12):** landed the two remaining attack-legality riders. Part A ŌĆö a per-token, this-turn *must-attack requirement*: new `combat_extras.must_attack: Vec<(ObjectId, PlayerId)>` (sibling of `goaded`, cleared at the next Untap), `Event::MustAttackDeclared`, and a `create_token.must_attack_defender` bool that emits one per minted token naming an opponent of the controller; enforced by a requirement loop in `Game::declare_attackers` mirroring the goad loop (CR 508.1a "if able"). Part B ŌĆö the vow restriction: new `CounterKind::Vow` (COUNT 3ŌåÆ4), a `Permanent::vow_protected: Option<PlayerId>` scalar, `Event::VowCountersPlaced`, and a new `Effect::PlaceVowCounters { filter }` run as Promise's `each_player_sacrifices` `then` ŌĆö it vow-marks every surviving creature (protected = the caster) and the restriction is read live in `declare_attackers` (attacker with a vow counter can't attack its `vow_protected` player), so removing the counter lifts it. Both events mirrored in `crates/schema` (public combat state, no redaction). **Fully faithful (note deleted):** promise_of_loyalty. **Trimmed:** furygale_flocking (residual: per-opponent scaling still flattened to 1v1 ŌĆö a different unlanded item; dropped the "forced-attack rider isn't modeled" clause). **Still blocked:** nils_discipline_enforcer (counter-scaled attack *tax* + per-player multi-target ŌĆö #68 X-in-costs + #102, out of scope). Do not mark #80 LANDED.

**Progress (2026-07-15):** nils_discipline_enforcer fully faithful ŌĆö per-player ability-controller-chosen up-to-one counter fan-out (#102) + counter-scaled per-attacker attack tax (this entry). New `Effect::CounterScaledAttackTax` (a fieldless `timing = "static"`) read in `Game::attack_tax_owed`: reworked to sum per (attacker, defender) pair, adding each such attacker's own counter count (`Game::total_counters`, CR 122.1 ŌĆö all counter kinds) for every defender-controlled counter-scaled taxer; a counterless attacker owes nothing. The flat `Effect::AttackTax` summand is behavior-preserving (full suite green). nils was the last card of this list. **#80 LANDED.**

### 81. `watch-trigger-arms` ŌĆö 7 cards, S ŌĆö **LANDED (2026-07-11, partial pool)**
