### 82. `nonmana-activation-costs` ŌĆö 6 cards, M ŌĆö **LANDED (2026-07-11)**
Non-mana cost flavors on activated/triggered abilities beyond sac-one/pay-life/remove-counters: mill-a-card (Millikin), sacrifice-two-creatures (Priest of Forgotten Gods), return-self-to-hand (Rootha), may-discard as a triggered-ability cost (Quintorius Chaser's +1; Conspiracy Theorist's "pay {1} and discard a card" ŌĆö reusing v1 #11's spell-side discard plumbing on the landed pay-or-decline trigger `Cost`), and exile-a-filtered-card-from-your-graveyard as a cost (Quintorius Loremaster). Sketch: extend `ActivationCost` / the trigger `PayCost` path arm by arm; each is one gate check + one payment event.
*Cards:* conspiracy_theorist, millikin, priest_of_forgotten_gods, quintorius_history_chaser, quintorius_loremaster, rootha_mercurial_artist

**Progress (2026-07):** 3 of 6 cards landed ŌĆö the paid-on-activation flavors. New `ActivationCost.return_self` (bool ŌĆö bounces the ability's own source on activation via the existing `ReturnedToHand`/`TokenCeasedToExist` events) and `ActivationCost.mill_self` (u8 ŌĆö mills the activator's own library, gated payable so an empty library can't pay it, CR 602.2b); `SacrificeCost::Creature` grew a `count: u8` (`sacrifice = { creature = { other = true }, count = 2 }`) so the activator names exactly N distinct controlled creatures, propagated by widening `Intent::{ActivateAbility,TakeAction}.sacrifice` from `Option<ObjectId>` to `Vec<ObjectId>`. **Faithful (notes deleted):** rootha_mercurial_artist (return-self), millikin (mill-a-card). **Trimmed:** priest_of_forgotten_gods ŌĆö "Sacrifice two other creatures" is now faithful; residual note is only the edict targeting each opponent rather than "any number of target players". **Still blocked:** quintorius_history_chaser + conspiracy_theorist (their "may discard a card. If you do, ŌĆ”" is an effect-internal optional sub-action, CR 608.2c, not an activation/trigger cost gate ŌĆö a distinct unlanded mechanism), quintorius_loremaster + conspiracy_theorist (also need #86 play-from-exile); the exile-a-graveyard-card-as-cost flavor never landed.

**Progress (2026-07-11):** 4 of 6 cards now landed. New `Effect::MayDiscard { then }` ŌĆö the effect-internal optional sub-action (CR 608.2c) the previous progress note flagged as unlanded: pauses on a `PendingChoice::MayDiscard` (empty hand skips straight past) so the controller may discard one card from hand; `then` runs only "if you do", reusing `Intent::ChooseSacrifices`'s "empty declines, one entry picks" wire shape exactly as `MaySacrifice`/`MayReturnFromGraveyard` do. **Fully faithful (note deleted):** quintorius_history_chaser ŌĆö its +1 is now `may_discard` with `then = [draw_cards 2, mill_self 1]`; its "whenever cards leave your graveyard, create a 3/2 Spirit" trigger also landed for free on the already-existing `Trigger::CardsLeaveYourGraveyard` (from #81), copied from quintorius_field_historian's identical ability. **Still blocked:** conspiracy_theorist's own may-discard loot still needs #86 play-from-exile for its second ability; quintorius_loremaster also needs #86; the exile-a-graveyard-card-as-cost flavor never landed. Do not mark #82 LANDED.

**Progress (2026-07-11, later same day):** quintorius_loremaster's dependency on #86 is now resolved ŌĆö see #86's progress note. Its end-step "exile target noncreature, nonland card from your graveyard" turned out not to need activation-cost plumbing at all: it's a triggered ability's own targeted effect step (`Effect::ExileTargetFromGraveyardWithThis`, CR 603, not a CR 602/118.9 cost), so it landed under #86 instead of here; #82's own remaining scope is unchanged (conspiracy_theorist's may-discard loot, still needing #86 play-from-exile for its second ability). Do not mark #82 LANDED.

**Progress (2026-07-11, closing slice):** conspiracy_theorist landed ŌĆö #82 is fully LANDED, 6 of 6 cards. Its "whenever this creature attacks, you may pay {1} and discard a card. If you do, draw a card" reuses the same `optional = true` + `[abilities.cost]` paid-trigger gate as `vanguard_of_the_restless`'s pay-{2}{W}-or-decline, resolving to `Effect::MayDiscard { then = [draw_cards 1] }`; its "whenever you discard one or more nonland cards, you may exile one of them ŌĆ” you may cast it this turn" copies `containment_construct`'s `you_discard` + `exile_from_graveyard_may_play` shape verbatim (the #86 play-from-exile prereq this card was blocked on). **Fully faithful (note deleted):** conspiracy_theorist, modulo three ponytail'd residuals left as gap notes on the card: (1) "pay {1} and discard" modeled as a paid gate then a separate may-discard rather than one all-or-nothing cost ŌĆö lets a player pay {1} and decline the discard, a strictly-dominated line no one takes; (2) `Trigger::YouDiscard` is unfiltered (fires on a discarded land too, strictly upside); (3) it fires once per discarded card rather than offering one "choose one of them" pick across a multi-card discard (unobservable for single-card discards, the only case this card's own loot produces).

**Progress (2026-07-15):** closed a per-card residual #82's own scope left open ŌĆö magma_opus's alternative "{U/R}{U/R}, Discard this card: Create a Treasure token." (not one of the 6 cards listed above; it surfaced only after #82 landed). New general primitive, the from-hand sibling of `CardDef::cycling` for a card whose hand-activated ability has an authored payload instead of cycling's fixed draw-1 (CR 113.6/602.5e): `CardDef::hand_ability: Option<HandActivatedAbility>` (`{ cost: Cost, effects: &'static [Effect] }`, `[hand_ability]`/`[hand_ability.cost]`/`[[hand_ability.effects]]` in TOML) plus `Game::activate_hand_ability`/`Intent::ActivateHandAbility`/`MeaningfulAction::ActivateHandAbility` ŌĆö a line-for-line clone of `Game::cycle`'s skeleton (priority check, hand+owner check, pay cost, discard via `MovedToGraveyard`, keep priority) except the payload is the card's own authored effect list, run inline through `Game::run` (the same resolving-ability executor a stack ability uses) rather than a hardcoded draw. ponytail-noted, mirroring cycling's own: resolved immediately rather than placed on the stack, since no pool card responds to this activation. **Fully faithful (first `approximates` sentence deleted):** magma_opus ŌĆö its "{U/R}{U/R}, Discard this card: Create a Treasure token." ability is now scripted (`[hand_ability]` with a hybrid `{U/R}{U/R}` cost and a `create_treasure` effect) and offered as a meaningful action from hand. Its sole remaining residual (unrelated to this slice, unchanged): the main spell's divided-damage clause targets creatures/planeswalkers only, not "any number of targets" broadly, since CR 601.2d's division bookkeeping (`DamageAssignment`) is keyed by permanent, not player ŌĆö a player-as-divided-damage-target is a separate, unbuilt increment.

### 83. `storm-copy-count` ŌĆö 6 cards, M ŌĆö **LANDED (2026-07)**
**Landed (all 6 faithful):** changing_loyalty (Replicate, CR 702.108), creative_technique + replication_technique (Demonstrate, CR 702.147), mirrorwing_dragon (spell-targets-this copy watch), ominous_harvest (permanents-died-this-turn count), plumb_the_forbidden (sacrifice-count). **Still blocked:** none.
Spell-copy with an `Amount`-scaled count and controller extensions on the landed `SpellCopied` + retarget machinery: Gravestorm (copy per permanent died this turn ŌĆö Ominous Harvest), copy-per-sacrificed-creature (Plumb the Forbidden, dep #92), copy-for-each-creature with per-copy retargeting (Mirrorwing), Replicate (copy per payment ŌĆö Changing Loyalty), and Demonstrate's opponent-controlled copy (Creative Technique). Sketch: an on-cast copy rider with an `Amount` count and a copy-controller field; the retarget choice per copy reuses `ChooseSpellTargets`.
*Cards:* changing_loyalty, creative_technique, mirrorwing_dragon, ominous_harvest, plumb_the_forbidden, replication_technique
**Landed:** `Effect::CopyThisSpell { count: Amount }` ŌĆö a resolution-time rider that mints `count` copies of the resolving spell itself, guarded so a copy never re-fires it (CR 706.9: a copy is never cast); all copies mint up front, then each copy's CR 707.10c retarget is queued one at a time through the existing `resolve_sequence` pause/resume via the internal `Effect::RetargetSpellCopy` so multiple retargeting copies don't clobber each other's `PendingChoice`. Two new `Amount`s feed the count: `SpellSacrificeCount` (creatures sacrificed to the spell's additional cost, reads the existing `spell_sacrifice_count` seam) and a game-wide `PermanentsDiedThisTurn` (new `Game::permanents_died_this_turn`, bumped on `Event::MovedToGraveyard` for a live battlefield `Object::Permanent` ŌĆö CR 700.4 "died", reset at Untap; counts every player's permanents, any type, unlike the per-controller-creature `CreaturesDiedThisTurn`). ponytail-noted: copies resolve as the spell's own trailing effect rather than CR 706.9's true copy-when-cast stack ordering, and a token's death isn't counted (goes through the ambiguous `TokenCeasedToExist`). **Faithful (notes deleted):** ominous_harvest, plumb_the_forbidden.
**Still blocked:** creative_technique + replication_technique (Demonstrate needs an optional "may copy" + choose-a-copy-controller decision), changing_loyalty (Replicate's copy-per-payment count), mirrorwing_dragon ("whenever a spell targets this, copy it" watch trigger) ŌĆö untouched.
**Progress (2026-07-14):** Landed the Demonstrate slice (CR 702.147), closing creative_technique and replication_technique. New `CardDef::demonstrate: bool` (a rules-keyword like `cascade`, fabricated at the same cast choke ŌĆö `Effect::Demonstrate { spell }` placed as a `TriggerGroup` above the cast spell). Resolution pauses on the existing `MayYesNo` "copy it?" surface; accepting mints one copy under the controller via `Game::mint_spell_copies` (its usual CR 707.10c retarget), then pauses the controller on a `PendingChoice::ChooseTarget` (reused, `TargetSpec::OpponentPlayer`-scoped legal list) to choose an opponent, who gets a second copy the same way. The two copies can't share one `mint_spell_copies` call (different controllers, one `ResolveCtx` per call), so a new `Game::pending_demonstrate_opponent_copy: Option<(PlayerId, ObjectId)>` defers the opponent's mint until the controller's own copy's retarget (if any) fully clears ŌĆö drained by `Game::resume_deferred_sequence`, the same "wait for the current pause" shape `pending_spell_finish` already uses. **Fully faithful (approximates trimmed to only the residual):** replication_technique (`approximates`/`ponytail:` deleted ŌĆö Demonstrate was its only gap). **Trimmed:** creative_technique ŌĆö Demonstrate clause deleted from `approximates`; residual is only the pre-existing "in a random order" deterministic-bottom-order stand-in (unrelated to Demonstrate). ponytail-noted on `Effect::Demonstrate`: the two copies mint/retarget sequentially (controller's fully resolved before the opponent's exists) rather than CR 707.10c's true simultaneous-objects-with-APNAP-ordered-retargets ŌĆö no pool Demonstrate card has a response window that would see the difference (mirrors `CopyThisSpell`'s existing approximation). **Still blocked, untouched ŌĆö do not conflate with Demonstrate, which is done:** changing_loyalty (Replicate's copy-per-payment count), mirrorwing_dragon ("whenever a spell targets this, copy it" watch trigger). Do not mark #83 LANDED ŌĆö 2 cards remain.
**Progress (2026-07-15):** Landed mirrorwing_dragon's watch trigger, closing that card. New `Trigger::SpellTargetsThisOnly { filter: SpellFilter }` (`timing = "spell_targets_this"`, reuses `cast_spell`'s `spell_filter` sibling) ŌĆö a `BecomesTargeted` twin narrowed to "only": fires off the same single-`Target` `Event::SpellCast` field, self-referential on the targeted permanent's own controller (`Game::queue_spell_targets_this_only_triggers`). New `Effect::CopyTriggeringSpellForEachOtherCreatureYouControl { triggering_spell }` (baked in by `fill_triggering_spell`, same context-fill machinery `CopyTriggeringSpell` uses): reads the *spell's own* controller off the still-live triggering spell (not this ability's controller ŌĆö "that player copies"), enumerates the spell's controller's other creatures the spell's own target spec could legally target (`Game::legal_targets_for`, honoring hexproof/protection), and mints one copy per creature via `SpellCopied` + a direct `SpellTargetsChosen` per copy ŌĆö set at mint rather than routed through the interactive `RetargetSpellCopy` pause, since the "different one of those creatures" assignment has no player choice to offer (CR 707.10c's per-copy retarget only exists for a chosen count, not an enumerated one). Two `ponytail:`s on the effect: "could target" is approximated as "a legal target of the spell's own spec, other than this permanent" (exact for the pool's single-target instant/sorcery consumers), and the distinct-target assignment is engine-chosen by enumeration order (mirrors `CopyThisSpell`'s existing retarget-ordering approximation). **Fully faithful (approximates/ponytail deleted):** mirrorwing_dragon. **Still blocked:** changing_loyalty (Replicate's copy-per-payment count) ŌĆö 1 card remains, do not mark #83 LANDED.
**Progress (2026-07-15, closing slice):** Landed Replicate's copy-per-payment count (CR 702.108), closing changing_loyalty. New `AdditionalCost::replicate: Option<&'static Cost>` (`[cost.additional.replicate]`, same `[cost]`-shaped sub-table as the landed `kicker`/`strive` siblings) plus a caster-declared pre-stack `Intent::Cast.replicate_count: u8` (mirroring `strive_count` end to end: folded into `Game::cast_cost` ŌĆö multiplied by the count directly, not `saturating_sub(1)`, since each replicate payment is a full extra instance of the cost, unlike Strive's "beyond the first" ŌĆö and recorded on the resulting `Spell::replicate_count`, read via the new `Game::spell_replicate_count`). Unlike Cascade/Demonstrate (rules-keyword *triggered* abilities fabricated at the cast choke), Replicate's copy doesn't use the stack (CR 702.108c) ŌĆö its copies mint directly inside `Game::cast_with_kind` right after `Event::SpellCast`, reusing the landed `Game::mint_spell_copies(Amount::Fixed(replicate_count), ...)` rider (same per-copy CR 707.10c `RetargetSpellCopy` pause `CopyThisSpell` uses). The pool's real work was CR 707.10a ŌĆö "a copy of a permanent spell becomes a token as it resolves" ŌĆö which nothing had exercised yet (every prior `mint_spell_copies` consumer copies an instant/sorcery): `Event::PermanentEntered`'s apply now reads the resolving spell's own `copy` flag and sets the entered `Permanent::token` from it (one shared choke for both the Creature/Enchantment/Artifact/Planeswalker and Aura resolution paths), so a copied permanent already rides every existing token-cease mechanism (dies/sacrifice/bounce/exile) for free. Three real gaps surfaced and fixed along the way, each was previously unreachable because no prior copy consumer targeted a permanent: (1) `Effect::RetargetSpellCopy`'s target-spec lookup only scanned for a `Timing::Spell` ability ŌĆö meaningless for an Aura, whose cast-target requirement is `CardKind::Aura`-derived, not effect-carried (CR 303.4a) ŌĆö switched to the general `Game::required_target` helper (already used by the original cast's own legality check), so a copied Aura now gets a real CR 707.10c retarget choice; (2) `resolve_spell`'s `CardKind::Aura` branch sent an illegal-retarget fizzle straight to `MovedToGraveyard` unconditionally ŌĆö a copy that fails to resolve must cease to exist instead (CR 707.10a/111.7, mirroring `finish_instant_sorcery_resolution`'s own copy guard), fixed with a `spell.copy` guard; (3) the state-based "unattached Aura" sweep (`Game::check_state_based_actions`) also routed every falling-off Aura through `graveyard_or_command` unconditionally ŌĆö a *token* Aura (a Replicate copy whose host died or was destroyed) needs the same `Permanent::token` branch every other token-leaves-the-battlefield path already has, fixed by checking `p.token` there too. Fixing (3) surfaced a second latent bug it depends on: `Trigger::EnchantedCreatureDies`/`AnEnchantedCreatureDies`'s shared `dying_creature_attachments` snapshot re-read a dying Aura's controller/def live at trigger-queue time (`self.controller_of(aura)`/`self.def_of(aura)`), which panics (or, behind the pre-existing "skip if `Object::Removed`" guard, silently drops the trigger) once a token Aura's own same-batch `TokenCeasedToExist` tombstones it straight to `Object::Removed` with no `Moved` lineage to follow (unlike an ordinary Aura's `MovedToGraveyard`, which still resolves post-move) ŌĆö fixed by widening the snapshot tuple to capture `(host, aura, controller, def)` at push time (when the Aura is still live) instead of re-deriving them later, and replacing the "is this object Removed" heuristic with the real CR 800.4a condition it was standing in for (`self.players[controller].lost`) so a vanished-but-legitimate token Aura's dies-trigger fires correctly instead of being conflated with "its owner left the game." **Fully faithful (approximates deleted):** changing_loyalty ŌĆö Replicate copies are token Auras with a real CR 707.10c retarget choice and full copied functionality (a copy attached to an opponent's creature steals it on death exactly like the original). ponytail-noted (mirrors kicker/strive precedent): the cost fold sums generic/colored/colorless pips only (no pool replicate cost carries a hybrid pip), and only a single replicate cost is modeled (Changing Loyalty is the pool's only replicate card). New reusable surface for any future replicate/permanent-copy card: `AdditionalCost::replicate`, `Intent::Cast.replicate_count`/`Spell::replicate_count`, and copied-permanent-spell ŌåÆ token resolution. **All 6 `storm-copy-count` cards are now faithful** (changing_loyalty, creative_technique, mirrorwing_dragon, ominous_harvest, plumb_the_forbidden, replication_technique) ŌĆö #83 promoted to LANDED.

### 84. `reveal-until` ŌĆö 6 cards, M ŌĆö **LANDED (2026-07)**
Reveal from the top of the library until a condition matches, then route: first nonland (Chaos Warp's replacement land check), an Aura card ŌåÆ hand/battlefield-attached (Songbird's Blessing), until X lands with a variable put-count (Open the Way), reveal-top-then-conditionally-deploy ("if it's a permanent card, put it onto the battlefield" ŌĆö Chaos Warp; Demonstrate hit ŌĆö Creative Technique), and reveal-top-and-branch engines (Goblin Guide's defender reveal, Keen Duelist's symmetric MV drain). Sketch: a bounded reveal loop variant of the landed `LookAtTop` with a stop predicate, revealed cards public, plus a conditional dest.
*Cards:* chaos_warp, creative_technique, goblin_guide, keen_duelist, open_the_way, songbirds_blessing
**Landed:** the count-1 slice ŌĆö a public reveal (new `Event::RevealedTopOfLibrary`, unlike `LookAtTop`'s private look). `Effect::RevealTopToHand { filter, defender }`: reveals the *defending* player's top card (read off the attack trigger's context, extended to carry `(attacker, defender)` for the self `Trigger::Attacks` too, not just the watch-others triggers) and routes it to hand if it matches `filter`, else it stays on top. `Effect::RevealTopAndDrainMutual` (`TargetSpec::OpponentPlayer`): the controller and the chosen opponent each reveal their top card, each loses life equal to the *other's* mana value, then each puts their own revealed card into hand (not a draw). **Faithful (notes deleted):** goblin_guide, keen_duelist. **Still blocked (notes untouched, no true reveal-until-predicate loop built ŌĆö count-1 only):** chaos_warp (also needs battlefieldŌåÆlibrary shuffle-into, #105), creative_technique (needs spell-copy, #83), open_the_way (needs X-scaling, #68/#89), songbirds_blessing (needs Aura re-attach, #79).
**Progress (2026-07-11):** landed the genuine reveal-until-a-count loop, scoped to open_the_way. New `Effect::RevealUntil { filter, count: Amount, matched_dest: SearchDest, matched_tapped: bool, rest_dest: RestDest }` (pure `execute_effect` arm ŌĆö fully deterministic given the library, no player choice): walks the controller's own top-of-library one card at a time, revealing each publicly (`Event::RevealedTopOfLibrary`) until `count` cards match `filter` or the library runs out (CR 120-style "as many as possible"); each match routes to `matched_dest` (`Battlefield` via the existing `Event::SearchedToBattlefield`, tapped per `matched_tapped`), every other revealed card goes to `rest_dest` (`RestDest::Bottom`, the enum `LookAtTop` already uses ŌĆö no new enum needed). New `Event::PutOnBottomOfLibrary { player, card }` for the non-matching reveals: a same-zone reorder, not a zone change (CR 400.7), so it reuses the card's existing object id rather than minting a new one the way `TuckedToLibrary` (graveyardŌåÆlibrary, a real zone change) does; schema-mirrored as public (the card was already revealed). "In a random order" is approximated as bottom-in-library-order, the same deterministic no-`rand` stand-in `select_from_top`'s `RestDest::Bottom` arm already uses (ponytail-noted on the card). **Fully faithful (approximates + ponytail block deleted):** open_the_way. **Still blocked, each behind a *different* prereq ŌĆö do not conflate with this landed reveal-until loop:** chaos_warp (needs a battlefieldŌåÆlibrary tuck, #105, *plus* a reveal-top-**one**-and-maybe-deploy shape, different from reveal-until-N), songbirds_blessing (reveal-until-an-Aura then attach it, #79's choose-host attach), creative_technique (reveal + spell-copy, #83). Do not mark #84 LANDED.
**Progress (2026-07-12):** chaos_warp's own reveal-top-one-and-maybe-deploy landed as part of closing #105's battlefieldŌåÆlibrary tuck (`Effect::ShuffleTargetPermanentIntoLibraryThenReveal` ŌĆö see #105's dated note for the full shape). **Fully faithful (approximates deleted):** chaos_warp. **Still blocked:** songbirds_blessing (needs Aura re-attach, #79), creative_technique (needs spell-copy, #83). Do not mark #84 LANDED.
**Progress (2026-07-12):** Landed the reveal-until-first-match-with-a-routed-pause slice, closing songbirds_blessing's and creative_technique's reveal-until cores. Two new sibling effects to the landed no-pause `RevealUntil` ŌĆö kept separate rather than widening it with a pause axis, since `RevealUntil` is deliberately deterministic and makes no player choice: `Effect::RevealUntilMayDeploy { filter }` (songbirds_blessing) and `Effect::RevealUntilExileCastFree { filter }` (creative_technique). Both walk the controller's own top-of-library one card at a time, bottoming every non-match via the same per-card loop shape `RevealUntil` uses, until the first card matching `filter` or the library runs out; a hit pauses instead of auto-routing. `RevealUntilMayDeploy` pauses on a new `PendingChoice::RevealedCardToBattlefieldOrHand` ŌĆö a single card, left unmoved on top of the library until answered: accepting routes it via the existing `Event::SearchedToBattlefield` (untapped), declining via `Event::SearchedToHand`. `RevealUntilExileCastFree` reuses #86's `PendingChoice::ChooseExiledDigToCastFree` outright (a single-candidate batch: `candidates = exiled = vec![hit]`), no new pending-choice needed. New `CardFilter::Nonland` (the inverse of `Land`). New `Effect::ShuffleLibrary` (TOML `shuffle_library`, untargeted, `&mut self`-only for the injected PRNG) precedes creative_technique's reveal-until step as its own `[[abilities.effects]]` in the same `Sequence` (CR 701.19's mandatory shuffle before the reveal). Found and fixed a pre-existing engine bug along the way, with a regression test: `Game::queue_permanent_enters_triggers` unconditionally read the live-only `self.permanent(entering)`, which panics when the entering permanent already left the battlefield in the same event batch's state-based sweep (CR 704's SBAs precede trigger placement) ŌĆö an unattached Aura (CR 704.5m) hits exactly this path; fixed to read it via `Game::as_permanent` instead. **Trimmed (each still carries a residual ŌĆö not fully faithful):** songbirds_blessing ŌĆö the reveal-until-Aura loop, the battlefield-or-hand pause, and the hand routing are all faithful now; the residual is CR 303.4f's attach-a-host step (#79's choose-host `PendingChoice`, unbuilt) ŌĆö an Aura accepted onto the battlefield this way enters unattached, which CR 704.5m makes illegal, so the very next state-based sweep immediately puts it into the graveyard (same residual armored_skyhunter's dig already carries). creative_technique ŌĆö the shuffle-then-reveal-until-nonland-exile-cast-free core is faithful now; the residual is Demonstrate (the copy-on-cast rider ŌĆö "you may copy it, if you do, choose an opponent to also copy it" ŌĆö a shared gap with replication_technique, not a reveal-until behavior, out of scope here).
**Landed:** the reveal-until capability is complete across every reveal-until shape (reveal-until-N, reveal-until-first-match with a routed battlefield/hand or exile-cast-free pause, reveal-top-one-and-deploy, reveal-and-branch). **Faithful (notes deleted):** goblin_guide, keen_duelist, open_the_way, chaos_warp. **Still blocked (notes trimmed to the residual, each gated on a *different* increment, not on reveal-until):** songbirds_blessing (Aura choose-host attach, #79 ŌĆö an accepted Aura enters unattached and CR 704.5m sweeps it to the graveyard), creative_technique (Demonstrate/spell-copy, #83).
**Progress (2026-07-13):** the deploy-time choose-host `PendingChoice::ChooseAttachHostForAura` landed (see #79's dated note), closing songbirds_blessing's attach-a-host residual ŌĆö an Aura accepted onto the battlefield off the reveal now pauses its controller to choose a legal host (CR 303.4f); with no legal host it stays unattached for CR 704.5m to sweep. **Trimmed (residual is now only the random-order stand-in ŌĆö `approximates` reduced to `"in a random order"` ŌåÆ deterministic bottom-order):** songbirds_blessing. Still blocked: creative_technique (Demonstrate/spell-copy, #83).

### 85. `cost-reduction-dynamic-2` ŌĆö 6 cards, M
Grow the landed `reduce_own_generic`/`ReduceSpellCost` pair: a `Condition` gate ("{2} less if you gained life this turn" ŌĆö Mortality Spear; the flag exists), `PerPermanentMatching` scaling (affinity for Auras ŌĆö Pearl-Ear; for planeswalkers ŌĆö Tomik), a summed-power amount ("{1} less per total power" ŌĆö Volcanic Salvo), a per-graveyard-card-type count (Furygale ŌĆö instant/sorcery cards in your graveyard), and a cast-zone predicate ("spells you cast from anywhere other than your hand cost {2} less" ŌĆö Advanced Reconstruction level 3; flashback/escape/impulse already carry their source zone).
*Cards:* advanced_reconstruction, furygale_flocking, mortality_spear, pearl_ear_imperial_advisor, tomik_wielder_of_law, volcanic_salvo

**Progress (2026-07):** 3 of 6 cards landed. New `Amount::TotalPowerYouControl` (`"total_power_you_control"`) and `Amount::IfCondition { condition, then }` (the `{ condition = ..., then = ... }` table form), both resolved through `reduce_own_generic`'s existing `resolve_amount` at cast time. Fully faithful (notes deleted): volcanic_salvo ("{X} less where X is total power of creatures you control"), mortality_spear ("{2} less if you gained life this turn" ŌĆö `{ condition = { type = "you_gained_life_this_turn" }, then = 2 }`). Trimmed: tomik_wielder_of_law ŌĆö affinity for planeswalkers is now faithful (`reduce_own_generic = { per_permanent = { types = ["planeswalker"] } }`); note trimmed to the residual punisher trigger (#91). **Still blocked:** pearl_ear_imperial_advisor (its "enchantment spells you cast have affinity for Auras" discounts *other* spells, needing a dynamic-`Amount` `reduce_spell_cost` + enchantment filter, not the self-reducer), advanced_reconstruction (cast-zone predicate, #133), furygale_flocking (per-graveyard-card-type count).

**Progress (2026-07-11):** 4 of 6 cards now landed. `Effect::ReduceSpellCost.amount` grew from a bare `u8` to a live `Amount`, resolved through the same `Game::resolve_amount` as `reduce_own_generic` (source = the reducer permanent, `x = 0`), clamped to `>= 0` and summed across every matching reducer in `Game::cost_reduction`. **Fully faithful (note trimmed):** pearl_ear_imperial_advisor ŌĆö "Enchantment spells you cast have affinity for Auras" is now `reduce_spell_cost` with `amount = { per_permanent = { subtypes = ["Aura"], controller = "you" } }` and `filter = "enchantment"`; its note is trimmed to only the residual "targets a modified permanent" draw trigger (dep #90's still-unlanded "modified" `PermanentFilter` predicate). **Still blocked:** furygale_flocking's graveyard instant/sorcery count turned out structural, not small ŌĆö `TypeSet`/`CardKind::types()` has no INSTANT/SORCERY bit, and `CardFilter::Permanent`/`PermanentWithManaValueAtMost`/`NonlandPermanentWithManaValueAtMost` (search-library filters used by several other cards) rely on `CardKind::Spell.types().is_empty()` to exclude instants/sorceries from "permanent" matches ŌĆö adding those bits would silently make every instant/sorcery match those "permanent" search filters too. Needs a graveyard-scoped spell-speed axis that doesn't touch `TypeSet`, not attempted this slice. advanced_reconstruction unchanged (cast-zone predicate, #133).

**Progress (2026-07-11):** 5 of 6 cards now landed. furygale_flocking's graveyard instant/sorcery count turned out not to need the `TypeSet` route the prior note flagged as structural ŌĆö a bespoke `Amount::InstantOrSorceryCardsInYourGraveyard` reads `CardKind::Spell` directly off each graveyard card (reusing the existing `Game::graveyard_cards` enumerator, no `TypeSet` bit touched, no risk to the `CardFilter::Permanent`-family search filters). Wired as `reduce_own_generic = "instant_or_sorcery_cards_in_your_graveyard"`, resolved through the same `Game::resolve_amount` as `total_power_you_control`. **Fully faithful (note trimmed):** furygale_flocking ŌĆö cost reduction is now exact; note trimmed to the still-flattened per-opponent token scaling and the unmodeled forced-attack rider. **Still blocked:** advanced_reconstruction unchanged (cast-zone predicate, #133).
**Progress (2026-07-15):** landed the "once-per-turn dynamic self-reducer" this section names but that none of its own 6 listed cards forced ŌĆö zimone_infinite_analyst (not one of the 6; a separate consumer of the same `ReduceSpellCost` machinery). New `Effect::ReduceSpellCost.first_x_spell_each_turn: bool` (`#[serde(default)]`) gates the reducer to the controller's first spell this turn matching `filter`, read in `Game::cost_reduction` off the already-existing `Player::x_spells_cast_this_turn` tally (no new per-turn state ŌĆö `cost_reduction` runs before the current cast's own tally bump, so a 0 reading means this cast is the turn's first). zimone_infinite_analyst is `reduce_spell_cost { amount = "per_counter_on_source", filter = "has_x", first_x_spell_each_turn = true }`, paired with its already-landed counter-trigger ability. **Fully faithful (note deleted):** zimone_infinite_analyst. ponytail: the gate is wired specifically to the {X}-spell tally (Zimone's only pool consumer, `filter = "has_x"`) rather than a general per-filter "first matching this turn" counter; a differently-filtered once-per-turn reducer needs its own per-turn tally. **#85 itself is NOT fully landed** ŌĆö advanced_reconstruction (this section's own 6th listed card) is still blocked on the unrelated cast-zone predicate (#133); do not mark #85 LANDED.

### 86. `free-cast-from-exile` ŌĆö 5 cards, M ŌĆö **LANDED (2026-07-12)**
The "may cast while exiled" generalization v1 #37 left open: a cast permission on source-linked exile piles checked in `Game::cast`'s `playable_zone`, with an expiry key ("this turn" / "for as long as it remains exiled") and a pay-nothing flavor (cast-without-paying-mana-cost ŌĆö Plargg's upkeep exile-and-cast, Loremaster's cast-from-exile ability, Herald of Amity's dig-and-cast-free Aura, Renegade Bull's exile-a-copy-then-cast-free). Conspiracy Theorist's discard-to-impulse-cast is the smallest slice. The impulse-play permission and `exiled_with` piles exist; this is the permission entry + free-cost flag.
*Cards:* conspiracy_theorist, herald_of_amity, plargg_and_nassari, quintorius_loremaster, renegade_bull

**Progress (2026-07-11):** the core pay-nothing permission landed, with quintorius_loremaster as its one faithful consumer. New `play_permissions.cast_from_exile_free: Vec<(ObjectId, PlayerId)>` (`state.rs`), distinct from the pre-existing `play_from_exile` (which still charges normal cost) ŌĆö checked in `playable_zone`'s `Zone::Exile` arm and forced to `Cost::FREE` in `cast_cost` (CR 118.5 "without paying its mana cost"), cleared unconditionally at cleanup (`Event::CastFromExileFreeEnded`, no `until_next_turn` extension needed yet). New `Effect::CastExiledWithThisFree` (Quintorius's activated ability) pauses on a `PendingChoice::ChooseExiledWithCardToCast` over the source's `exiled_with` pile ŌĆö "up to one," mirroring `CashOutExiledWithThis`/`ChooseExiledWithCard` exactly, except accepting grants the free-cast permission instead of cashing the card out (it stays in the pile). Also landed, as a prerequisite: `Effect::ExileTargetFromGraveyardWithThis` (a targeted counterpart to `ExileDiscardedWithThis`, hardcoding a `noncreature_nonland` `CardFilter` target since the target restriction is fixed) for Quintorius's end step ŌĆö this turned out to be a plain triggered-ability target step, not an activation cost, so it also resolves #82's still-open quintorius_loremaster item (#82 stays not-LANDED; see its own note). **Fully faithful (note trimmed):** quintorius_loremaster ŌĆö residual is only the activated ability's "if that spell would be put into a graveyard, put it on the bottom of its owner's library instead" replacement rider (a replacement effect scoped to one cast object, #128 territory), untouched.
**Still blocked, each behind a *different* unlanded prereq ŌĆö do not conflate with the free-cast permission itself, which is now done:** conspiracy_theorist (needs a "whenever you discard" trigger paired with *normal-cost* impulse play, not free-cast ŌĆö a different permission entirely); herald_of_amity (needs a filtered dig-8-and-cast-an-Aura reveal effect + a dynamic-Aura-count pump, neither built); plargg_and_nassari (needs each-player-exile-from-library + opponent-chooses, #107); renegade_bull (needs copy-a-graveyard-instant/sorcery, #83's copy machinery, extended to a graveyard source). Do not mark #86 LANDED.
**Progress (2026-07-12):** Landed the dig-and-cast-an-Aura-free slice, herald_of_amity as its sole consumer. New `Effect::ExileTopCastMatchingFree { count: u32, filter: CardFilter }` (TOML `exile_top_cast_matching_free`) exiles the top `count` library cards face-up via a new `Event::ExiledFromLibraryToChooseCastFree` (mirrors `ExiledFromLibraryMayPlay`'s zone-move/library-retain shape but attaches no play permission), then pauses on a new `PendingChoice::ChooseExiledDigToCastFree` ŌĆö "up to one" over the subset matching `filter`, mirroring `ChooseExiledWithCardToCast`'s public (non-`private_items`) exile-zone visibility. Unlike that sibling, answering here also sweeps every *other* card in the exiled batch (non-matching, or simply not chosen) to the bottom of the library via `Event::TuckedToLibrary` (its `create_object`-based apply is zone-agnostic, so the existing graveyardŌåÆlibrary event reuses cleanly for exileŌåÆlibrary too) ŌĆö a genuine second rule that `ChooseExiledWithCardToCast`'s pile doesn't have (its non-chosen candidates just stay put). No candidates matching `filter` skips the pause entirely and bottoms the whole batch immediately (mirrors `begin_cast_exiled_with_this_free`'s empty-pile no-op). New `CardFilter::Aura` (TOML `"aura"`, the `AuraOrEquipment` reader minus the Equipment half). The attack pump was pure authoring, no engine change: `power`/`toughness = { per_permanent = { subtypes = ["Aura"], controller = "you" } }` on the already-landed `Effect::PumpSelfUntilEndOfTurn`, the same shape #95's Eidolon of Countless Battles/Sage's Reverie already prove. herald_of_amity is now fully faithful (`approximates` deleted; two `ponytail:` code comments remain: the free cast is offered at a later priority window than mid-resolution, and "random order" for the bottomed rest is the deterministic library-order stand-in every impulse-dig effect in this pool uses). **Still blocked, unchanged prereqs:** plargg_and_nassari (#107, each-player-exile-from-library + opponent-chooses), renegade_bull (#83 extended to a graveyard source, copy-a-graveyard-instant/sorcery). conspiracy_theorist untouched this slice (its own distinct normal-cost impulse-play permission). Do not mark #86 LANDED ŌĆö 2 cards remain.
**Progress (2026-07-12):** Landed renegade_bull's exile-a-copy-then-cast-free attack trigger, the #83-extended-to-a-graveyard-source slice. New `Effect::ExileTargetGraveyardSpellAndCopyFree { filter: CardFilter }` (TOML `exile_target_graveyard_spell_and_copy_free`) ŌĆö a targeted counterpart to `ExileTargetFromGraveyardWithThis` with an authored `filter` instead of a fixed one ŌĆö exiles the "up to one" chosen graveyard target, then mints one free copy of it onto the stack via `Game::mint_spell_copies` (the same Storm/Twincast core `Effect::CopyThisSpell` uses), with the just-exiled card standing in for a live spell as the copy source. `mint_spell_copies` could not take an arbitrary `CardDef` source outright ŌĆö its `Event::SpellCopied` apply arm hard-required a live `Object::Spell` (`self.spell(original)`) ŌĆö so this slice widened that one apply arm (`apply.rs`) to also accept an `Object::Card` source (graveyard/exile), defaulting the fields a bare card doesn't carry (targets/x/modes/flashback/escape/sacrifice_count/kicked) the same way `PreparedSpellCast`'s from-a-`CardDef` mint already does; behavior for every existing live-spell `SpellCopied` caller (Twincast, storm, Gravestorm) is unchanged. That widening is exactly the reusable primitive #86's own brief flagged for surge_to_victory's copy clause once that card is in scope ŌĆö note left here for whoever picks it up. renegade_bull's attack trigger is now scripted (`approximates` trimmed to its residuals): the mint routes through `Event::SpellCopied`, so only Magecraft triggers fire for the free copy (CR 707.10's "cast or copy" watch), not a general "whenever you cast a spell" trigger ŌĆö Renegade Bull's own first ability (a `Trigger::CastSpell`, not Magecraft) does not refire off its own free copy; and the effect's fixed `min:1` target count models "up to one target"/"you may cast" as mandatory once a legal target exists (no decline). **Still blocked:** plargg_and_nassari (#107, each-player-exile-from-library + opponent-chooses) is the only card left in #86. Do not mark #86 LANDED ŌĆö 1 card remains.
**Progress (2026-07-12) ŌĆö #86 LANDED:** plargg_and_nassari's upkeep exile-and-cast landed as part of #107 (`opponent-chooses`), consuming the #86 free-cast permission (`Event::CastFromExileFreePermissionGranted`) for the "cast up to two ŌĆ” without paying their mana costs" clause. All five cards now script their cast-from-exile-without-paying mechanic; the residual `approximates` remaining on quintorius_loremaster (#128 replacement rider), renegade_bull (#83 Magecraft-only copy nuance), and plargg_and_nassari (#107's next-opponent / later-priority-window ponytails) are all outside #86's free-cast scope. #86 is complete.
**Progress (2026-07-15, renegade_bull closing slice):** Closed renegade_bull's own residual left by the 2026-07-12 note above ŌĆö its attack trigger's free copy now fires real "whenever you cast" watchers, including its own +X/+0. `Effect::ExileTargetGraveyardSpellAndCopyFree` renamed to `Effect::ExileTargetGraveyardSpellCastFree` (TOML `exile_target_graveyard_spell_cast_free`, sole consumer renegade_bull) and repointed off `Game::mint_spell_copies` onto the #86 free-cast-permission primitive: it exiles the chosen graveyard card, then pushes `Event::CastFromExileFreePermissionGranted` for it directly (no pending choice needed ŌĆö the target is already the ability's own chosen target), the same event `cast_exiled_with_this_free` (Quintorius) grants. The controller now genuinely *casts* the exiled card at their next opportunity via the ordinary `Intent::Cast` free-cast-from-exile path (`cast.rs`'s `may_cast_from_exile_free` check, `Cost::FREE`), so it's a real `Event::SpellCast` ŌĆö Renegade Bull's own `Trigger::CastSpell` ability fires off it (+X/+0, X = the cast spell's mana value) and so does every other "whenever you cast an instant or sorcery" watcher on the battlefield, not just Magecraft. Also closed the "up to one target"/"you may cast" mandatory approximation the 2026-07-12 note flagged: the effect gained a `count: TargetCount` field (`#[serde(default)]`, `{1,1}`; Renegade Bull authors `{0,1}`) ŌĆö reusing the existing `ChooseTarget { optional }` pending-choice plumbing (`min == 0` already wires an optional pause there) ŌĆö so the controller may now decline the graveyard target outright even with a legal one available, and separately may simply not act on the granted free-cast permission ("you may cast" falls out for free once casting is the controller's own later choice rather than an automatic mint). **Fully faithful (`approximates` deleted):** renegade_bull. `ponytail:` left on the effect: CR 707.10c's literal reading mints a copy and casts *that*; this casts the exiled card itself instead (the same "cast that card" shape `cast_exiled_with_this_free`/`exile_top_cast_matching_free` already use for their own free casts) ŌĆö unobservable for this pool, since nothing reads the resolved spell's post-resolution zone (a true copy ceases to exist there; the exiled original goes to its owner's graveyard normally instead). No other #86 card touched; #86 stays LANDED.

### 87. `aura-lifecycle-payoffs` ŌĆö 5 cards, M ŌĆö **LANDED (2026-07)**
The unlanded v1 #43 halves on the landed `EnchantedCreatureDies` snapshot machinery: `Trigger::ThisAuraLeaves` / Aura-put-into-graveyard ("when this is put into a graveyard from the battlefield, return it to hand" ŌĆö Fallen Ideal; "sacrifice it when this leaves" ŌĆö Animate Dead's rider), and host-dies look-back payoffs acting on "that card": reanimate the dying host (Gift of Immortality, with #74's next-end-step return), return this Aura from the graveyard attached to a new creature (Ghoulish Impetus, dep #79), and Changing Loyalty's reanimate-under-your-control.
*Cards:* animate_dead, changing_loyalty, fallen_ideal, ghoulish_impetus, gift_of_immortality
**Landed:** `Trigger::ThisAuraLeaves` (TOML timing `"this_put_into_graveyard"`) ŌĆö a self-referential, permanent-kind-agnostic twin of `Trigger::Dies`, fired off `Event::MovedToGraveyard`/`Event::TokenCeasedToExist`, guarded (via `BatchTriggerScratch::permanents_put_into_graveyard_from_battlefield`, captured at `apply.rs`'s `MovedToGraveyard` choke point) to objects that were a live battlefield `Object::Permanent` immediately before the move, so a milled/discarded copy of the same card does not fire it. Reuses the existing `Effect::ReturnThisToHand`. fallen_ideal's return-to-hand rider is now faithful; its `approximates` is trimmed to only the still-dropped granted activated ability (#123).
**Landed (2026-07, reanimate-dying-enchanted-creature slice):** `Effect::ReanimateDyingEnchantedCreature { under_owner }` (TOML `reanimate_dying_enchanted_creature`) ŌĆö a `TriggerContext::dying_enchanted_creature` look-back payoff off the already-landed `Trigger::EnchantedCreatureDies`, reanimating the specific creature the Aura was attached to when it died ("that card", CR 603.10a last-known information) under either the ability's own controller (`under_owner = false` ŌĆö changing_loyalty's "under your control") or the card's owner (`under_owner = true` ŌĆö gift_of_immortality's "under its owner's control"); guard-returns if that card no longer sits in a graveyard (exiled in response). Shares its ETB/event plumbing with `Effect::ReanimateToBattlefield` via a factored `Game::reanimate_event` core. changing_loyalty is now faithful (its former continuous-control-Aura approximation is replaced with the real dies-trigger; `approximates` trimmed to only the unlanded Replicate rider, #83). gift_of_immortality's reanimate clause is now faithful; `approximates` trimmed to only its second sentence (return this Aura to the battlefield attached to that creature at the next end step ŌĆö needs a graveyard-Aura-return-attached-to-a-specific-creature delayed effect, a separate unlanded primitive; #74's next-end-step delay alone isn't enough).
**Still blocked:** animate_dead's "sacrifice it when this leaves" needs a leaves-*any*-zone thread (not just graveyard-from-battlefield) plus host-reference plumbing to act on the enchanted creature.
**Progress (2026-07-13):** ghoulish_impetus landed ŌĆö see #74/#79's 2026-07-13 notes for the mechanism (`Effect::ReturnThisAuraFromGraveyardAttachedToChosenHost`/`ScheduleReturnThisAuraFromGraveyardAttachedToChosenHost`, reusing #79's `ChooseAttachHostForAura`). **Faithful (note deleted):** ghoulish_impetus. **Still blocked:** animate_dead's "sacrifice it when this leaves" (unchanged, above) is the only card left on #87's list.
**Progress (2026-07-15):** animate_dead landed ŌĆö **#87 is now LANDED**, every listed card is faithful (to its established residual). Part A, the "-1/-0" static, was free: a second `[[abilities]] timing = "static"` with the already-landed `grant_to_attached { power = -1, toughness = 0 }` (`Amount::Fixed` already accepts negative literals, screams_from_within precedent ŌĆö no engine change). Part B is the real work: a new leaves-to-*any*-zone self-trigger, distinct from `Trigger::ThisAuraLeaves` (which stays graveyard-only, Fallen Ideal's own semantics untouched). New `Trigger::ThisPermanentLeavesBattlefield` (TOML `this_leaves_battlefield`) fires off `MovedToGraveyard`/`MovedToExile`/`ReturnedToHand`/`TuckedToLibrary`/`TokenCeasedToExist` ŌĆö a new `BatchTriggerScratch::permanents_left_battlefield: Vec<(ObjectId, Option<ObjectId>)>` captures `(pre-move id, `Game::attached_to` host)` at each of those `Game::apply` exit choke points, mirroring exactly where/how `permanents_put_into_graveyard_from_battlefield` is populated (CR 603.10a last-known information, read before the exit tears the attachment down). A new `Game::queue_leaves_battlefield_triggers` helper (triggers.rs) looks the exiting object up in that scratch and fires the trigger with the captured host threaded into a new `TriggerContext::left_battlefield_host: Option<ObjectId>`. New `Effect::SacrificeEnchantedCreature { creature: Option<ObjectId> }` (`#[serde(skip)]`, baked from `ctx.left_battlefield_host` via a new `fill_left_battlefield_host` contextualize-effect hook, mirroring `fill_dying_enchanted_creature`) resolves by reusing the existing sacrifice choke (`Game::sacrifice_event` + `Event::Sacrificed`, `by` = the *creature's own* controller, not the ability's ŌĆö CR "that creature's controller sacrifices it") with the same guard-return shape as `Effect::SacrificeObject`: no-op if the context never captured a host, or if that creature no longer sits on the battlefield. One non-obvious wrinkle surfaced and fixed: the new `MovedToExile`/`ReturnedToHand`/`TuckedToLibrary` trigger-scan arm needs the same `Object::Removed` guard the `MovedToGraveyard` arm already carries (CR 800.4a ŌĆö a card whose owner leaves the game in the same SBA sweep is already gone by the time triggers scan the batch; caught by the pre-existing `dirgur_does_not_prepare_on_flashback_instant` regression test, which exercises a flashback spell's own post-resolution exile coinciding with an empty-library loss). Also surfaced (documented, not a bug): animate_dead is typed `enchantment` not `aura` kind (the established reanimate-on-ETB approximation), so CR 704.5m's Aura-orphan state-based action doesn't apply to it ŌĆö when its host dies first, it merely becomes unattached and stays on the battlefield rather than falling off to the graveyard; the `animate_dead_no_op_if_host_already_gone` test exercises the resulting fizzle path (a host-less `SacrificeEnchantedCreature`) rather than the SBA-orphan path the brief sketched, since that path doesn't arise for this card. `approximates` trimmed to only the reanimate-on-ETB residual ("enchant creature card in a graveyard" approximated by reanimate-on-ETB rather than selecting a graveyard card at cast). **Faithful (note trimmed):** animate_dead.
**Progress (2026-07-15):** closed animate_dead's remaining "enchant creature card in a graveyard" residual ŌĆö the graveyard target is now chosen AT CAST (CR 303.4a/601.2c, respondable), not a fresh pick after the Aura's already on the battlefield. New `CardDef.enchant_graveyard: bool` (TOML `enchant_graveyard = true`) ŌĆö the graveyard-card twin of `enchant`'s battlefield-permanent Aura target ŌĆö makes `Game::required_target` report `TargetSpec::CreatureCardInAnyGraveyard` for the card at cast, same as any other Aura's enchant-subject requirement. The chosen target is locked onto the entering permanent as a new `Permanent::cast_time_enchant_target: Option<ObjectId>` (`Event::PermanentEntered`'s apply arm, mirroring the existing `entered_with_x` "read the spell before it's gone" idiom ŌĆö the `Spell` object is destroyed by the time the card's own `etb` ability resolves). A new `TargetSpec::ThisAurasGraveyardTarget` (TOML `"this_auras_graveyard_target"`) reads that captured id back as a **fixed reference** ŌĆö the same no-pause, no-shroud/hexproof-check treatment `"this"`/`"enchanted_creature"` already get in `Game::place_targeted_ability` and `Game::legal_targets_for` ŌĆö so the card's `reanimate_to_battlefield` effect places straight onto the stack with the cast-time choice already fixed, empty (CR 603.3c: ability dropped) if that card has since left the graveyard. `Game::resolve_spell` gained a CR 608.2b/303.4f-style fizzle re-check scoped to `enchant_graveyard` cards (the pool's only non-Aura-kind permanent with a cast-time target): if the chosen graveyard card is exiled in response before Animate Dead resolves, the Aura goes straight to the graveyard rather than entering unattached. Kind stays `enchantment`, not `aura` (per the brief: the `CardKind::Aura` resolution path expects an existing battlefield host to attach to, which a graveyard card isn't yet) ŌĆö `approximates` trimmed to that residual only (kind tag + the "loses/gains enchant ability" self-rewrite modeled implicitly as staying attached). **animate_dead is now fully faithful to its established residual** (the kind-tag note is the only thing left, matching the brief's allowed trim). New engine tests: `animate_dead_targets_graveyard_creature_at_cast` (no-target cast is illegal; the chosen target causes no `PendingChoice` at cast or at ETB placement), `animate_dead_fizzles_if_target_exiled_in_response` (CR 608.2b). `ponytail:` narrow single-card scope on both the new `enchant_graveyard` field and `ThisAurasGraveyardTarget` ŌĆö the pool has exactly one Aura whose enchant subject is a graveyard card.

### 88. `token-entry-riders` ŌĆö 5 cards, M ŌĆö **LANDED (2026-07-15)**
Entry riders on token creation and `CreateTokenCopy` (which landed with fixed count and plain entry): enters tapped-and-attacking (myriad ŌĆö Redoubled Stormsinger; Combat Calligrapher's Inkling, which also enters under the *attacking player's* control ŌĆö extend `TokenController` with the trigger's subject player and hook the declared-attack state mid-combat), gains haste (Rionya), and copying the set of tokens that entered this turn (dep #70's timestamp). Pairs with #74 for the exile/sacrifice-at-end-step cleanup.
*Cards:* combat_calligrapher, muddle_the_ever_changing, redoubled_stormsinger, rionya_fire_dancer, twinflame
**Progress (2026-07-11):** the "gains haste" rider landed for `Effect::CreateTokenCopy` ŌĆö a `haste: bool` (`#[serde(default)]`) that, when set, pushes an until-EOT `Event::TempBoost { keywords: &[Keyword::Haste] }` per minted token (reusing the existing keyword-union event, no schema change). **Fully faithful (note deleted):** determined_iteration. **Still blocked:** the tapped-and-attacking/myriad/attacking-player-controller half (combat_calligrapher, muddle_the_ever_changing, redoubled_stormsinger, twinflame) is untouched ŌĆö needs `TokenController`'s attacking-player extension and mid-combat attack-state hookup, not attempted this slice. rionya_fire_dancer also wants "gains haste" but is blocked on begin-combat-cast tracking + variable-P/T (#89), unrelated prereqs, not this rider. Do not mark #88 LANDED.
**Progress (2026-07-11):** landed the tapped-and-attacking/attacking-player-controller slice, scoped to combat_calligrapher only. New `Effect::CreateToken.enters_tapped_and_attacking: bool` (TOML, `#[serde(default)]` false) plus an internal (never TOML-authored, `#[serde(skip)]`) `attacking_context: Option<(PlayerId, PlayerId)>` baked from `TriggerContext::attack` by a new `contextualize_effect` `CreateToken` arm at trigger placement ŌĆö the same "watch-others payload fill" shape `RevealTopToHand`/`DefendingPlayerSacrifices` already use. At resolution, a `Some(attacking_context)` overrides the `TokenController` recipient match (CR 111.4: minted under the *attacking* player) and each minted token gets a `Tapped` event plus a new `Event::TokenEnteredAttacking { token, defender }` (pushes into `combat.attackers`/`attack_targets`, mirroring `AttackerDeclared`'s apply arm). `TokenEnteredAttacking` deliberately carries no trigger-scan arm ŌĆö CR 508.4, a token put onto the battlefield attacking was never declared as an attacker, so reusing `AttackerDeclared` here would re-fire Combat Calligrapher and infinite-loop; the omission is the fix (regression-tested: exactly one token mints, no loop). Schema mirror added (`VisibleEvent::TokenEnteredAttacking` + projection arm; combat state is public, no redaction). **Fully faithful (note deleted):** combat_calligrapher. **Still blocked, untouched:** redoubled_stormsinger (myriad copy set, needs #70's entered-this-turn permanent-filter timestamp axis too), twinflame (Strive escalating per-target cost, #85), muddle_the_ever_changing (become-a-copy-until-EOT, #127), rionya_fire_dancer (begin-combat spells-cast count + temporary copies, #89/#83). Do not mark #88 LANDED.
**Progress (2026-07-12):** landed twinflame's `haste`/`sacrifice_at_next_end_step` riders on its existing `create_token_copy` (already-landed `Effect::CreateTokenCopy` fields ŌĆö no engine change) and rionya_fire_dancer's whole begin-combat trigger. New `Player::instants_and_sorceries_cast_this_turn: u32` tally (sibling of `greatest_instant_or_sorcery_mana_value_cast_this_turn`: bumped in the `Event::SpellCast` apply arm's existing instant-or-sorcery guard, reset at Untap; a copied spell doesn't bump it, same "cast" boundary as the mv tally) plus a new `Amount::OnePlusInstantsAndSorceriesCastThisTurn` (TOML `"one_plus_instants_and_sorceries_cast_this_turn"`, a live read like the mv `Amount`, `tally + 1`; ponytail: the baked "one plus" is Rionya-specific ŌĆö split into a raw count + successor combinator if a second card needs a different offset). rionya_fire_dancer's ability is `timing = "begin_combat"` + `create_token_copy { target = { permanent = { types = "creature", controller = "you", other = true } }, count = "one_plus_instants_and_sorceries_cast_this_turn", haste = true, sacrifice_at_next_end_step = true }` ŌĆö `other = true` excludes Rionya herself from her own "another target creature you control," and `begin_combat` is already controller-scoped (no intervening-if needed, unlike Rootha's conditional trigger). **Fully faithful (note deleted):** rionya_fire_dancer. **Trimmed to its Strive residual only (multi-target/escalating-cost, #85 territory):** twinflame ŌĆö haste and the end-step exile are now faithful. **Still blocked, untouched:** redoubled_stormsinger (needs #70's entered-this-turn timestamp for its myriad copy set), muddle_the_ever_changing (#127 become-a-copy). Do not mark #88 LANDED.
**Progress (2026-07-14):** landed redoubled_stormsinger ŌĆö an assembly of already-landed pieces, no new prereq. New single-purpose `Effect::CopyEachEnteredThisTurnTokenTappedAttacking { attacking_context }` (no target ŌĆö enumerates internally): `attacking_context: Option<(PlayerId, PlayerId)>` is filled by a new `contextualize_effect` arm from `TriggerContext::attack` at trigger placement, the same "watch payload fill" shape `CreateToken.attacking_context` (#88's combat_calligrapher slice) already uses, paired with `timing = "attacks"` (`Trigger::Attacks`, already self-referential and already populates `ctx.attack`, so no `triggers.rs` change was needed). At resolution it scans the attacking player's own battlefield for `token && creature && controller_you && entered_this_turn` (the already-landed `PermanentFilter.entered_this_turn` axis, #70) and, per match, mints a copy reusing `CreateToken`'s tapped-and-attacking apply path (`Event::Tapped` + `Event::TokenEnteredAttacking`, never `AttackerDeclared` ŌĆö CR 508.4, so a minted copy can't re-trigger Redoubled itself; regression-tested) and schedules `CreateTokenCopy`'s `sacrifice_at_next_end_step` delayed trigger (`Event::DelayedTriggerScheduled` ŌåÆ `Effect::SacrificeObject` at `Step::End`) verbatim. No schema change (`Effect` is card-dsl-only; the events it emits were already wire-mirrored by the combat_calligrapher slice). **Fully faithful (note deleted):** redoubled_stormsinger. This also clears redoubled_stormsinger off #74's still-blocked list (its delayed sacrifice-at-next-end-step is the same already-landed `Step::End` delayed-trigger machinery #74 covers). **Still blocked:** muddle_the_ever_changing ŌĆö its Magecraft "becomes a copy of another target creature you control ... and gains myriad" needs #127 (become-a-copy-until-EOT), an XL, unbuilt prereq. Do not mark #88 LANDED ŌĆö one card remains.
**Progress (2026-07-15):** landed muddle_the_ever_changing, this entry's last card, now that #127 (become-a-copy-until-EOT) is built. Two new effects on the landed `BecameCopy`/`ChooseTarget` substrate: `Effect::BecomeCopyOfTargetCreatureGainingMyriad { target }` ŌĆö a real CR 601.2c target (not a resolution-time pause; "up to one" is `optional = true` on the magecraft ability, the same shape Skyclave Apparition's "up to one target" already uses) that on resolution emits an until-EOT `BecameCopy` plus an until-EOT `myriad` keyword grant via `TempBoost` (the same "gains a keyword" shape `Game::answer_enter_as_copy`'s `gains_haste` rider uses) ŌĆö and `Effect::MyriadTokenCopies`, the myriad payload itself: never TOML-authored, synthesized by a new `Game::queue_myriad_triggers` off a new `Keyword::Myriad` the same way Prowess's pump is synthesized from `Keyword::Prowess` (`Game::queue_prowess_triggers`). For each opponent other than the defending player it mints a tapped-and-attacking token copy of the attacker's current characteristics (`Event::TokenCreated`/`Tapped`/`TokenEnteredAttacking`, never `AttackerDeclared` ŌĆö CR 508.4, so a minted copy can't re-trigger myriad; regression-tested, same pattern as combat_calligrapher/redoubled_stormsinger), reusing `Game::token_count_after_replacements` for Doubling Season, and schedules the token's exile at the *true* end of combat via `Event::DelayedTriggerScheduled { fire_at: Step::EndCombat }` ŌĆö `Step::EndCombat` was already a `fire_delayed_triggers` boundary (Decayed's own sacrifice uses it), so no new drain site was needed and no residual end-step-vs-end-of-combat note is required. New engine tests: `muddle_becomes_copy_of_chosen_creature_until_end_of_turn_on_magecraft`, `muddle_magecraft_declined_no_copy`, `muddle_copy_has_myriad_mints_tapped_attacking_copies_per_opponent`, `muddle_myriad_tokens_exiled_at_end_of_combat`. **This lands #88 ŌĆö all 5 cards (combat_calligrapher, muddle_the_ever_changing, redoubled_stormsinger, rionya_fire_dancer, twinflame) are now faithful** (twinflame's own Strive residual cleared separately under #85, wave 130). **#88 `token-entry-riders` LANDED (2026-07-15).**

### 89. `variable-pt-tokens` ŌĆö 5 cards, M ŌĆö **LANDED (2026-07-12)**
Token base P/T and enters-with-counters set from a dynamic `Amount` at creation, routed through the counter-replacement pipeline: Manaform Hellkite's X/X Dragon Illusion (X = the cast spell's MV, dep #65's context read), Rootha's X/X off spells-cast-this-turn, Fractal Harness / Lattice Library's variable-counter 0/0 Fractals (which die without their counters ŌĆö the SBA sweep already handles that), and Oversimplify's per-player Fractal with counters equal to each player's exiled power.
*Cards:* fractal_harness, lattice_library, manaform_hellkite, oversimplify, rootha_mastering_the_moment
**Progress (2026-07-11):** landed the enters-with-*counters* slice only (not base-P/T-set-from-Amount): `Effect::CreateToken` gained `enters_with: Amount` (TOML `enters_with`, `#[serde(default)]` zero ŌĆö behavior-preserving), applied to each minted token via `Game::counters_after_replacements` (CR 614 doublers/Hardened Scales apply) in a new `Game::resolve_effect` special case, since placing counters needs the token already in game state (`execute_effect` is pure `&self` and can't apply mid-resolution). `fill_cast_mana_value` now also fills `CreateToken.enters_with`. Also fixed a latent gap this surfaced: `Trigger::Magecraft` never threaded `TriggerContext::cast_mana_value` (only the general `CastSpell` form did), so `Amount::TriggeringSpellManaValue` silently resolved to 0 inside a Magecraft ability ŌĆö added `Game::queue_magecraft_triggers` (mirrors `queue_controller_triggers` but injects `cast_mana_value`), wired at both the cast (`Event::SpellCast`) and copy (`Event::SpellCopied`) trigger sites. **Fully faithful (note trimmed to its unrelated residual):** deekah_fractal_theorist ŌĆö the Magecraft "create a 0/0 ŌĆ” Fractal ŌĆ” put X +1/+1 counters on it" is exact; residual is only the dropped `{3}{U}: target creature token can't be blocked this turn` (needs a grant-unblockable-until-turn effect, not this slice ŌĆö only a static Unblockable keyword exists, #103). **Still blocked, untouched, notes left as-is:** manaform_hellkite and rootha_mastering_the_moment (need base-P/T-**set**-from-Amount for an X/X body, not counters ŌĆö a different `Effect`/static surface ŌĆö plus a delayed-exile-at-next-end-step for Manaform Hellkite and a "greatest MV among instants/sorceries cast this turn" `Amount` + begin-combat-if-cast trigger for Rootha); lattice_library (needs study counters, #75, + a first-{X}-spell-each-turn cast trigger, #67/#68); oversimplify (needs a *per-player* token/counters scope ŌĆö this slice is a single shared `Amount`, not per-player); fractal_harness (judgment call: left entirely as-is rather than partially scripting the counter half ŌĆö its ETB also needs equipment self-attach-to-minted-token, unbuilt, and the attack-trigger "double the counters," unbuilt; scripting only the counters would leave a non-functional Equipment).
**Progress (2026-07-11):** Landed the base-P/T-**set**-from-Amount slice (the genuine X/X body, distinct from `enters_with`'s counters). New `Effect::CreateToken.set_base_pt: Option<Amount>` (TOML `set_base_pt`, `#[serde(default)]` `None` ŌĆö behavior-preserving): resolved in the `CreateToken` execute arm (pure `&self`, no game-state dependency like `enters_with` needs) and baked straight into the minted def's `CardKind::Creature { power, toughness, .. }` before any tokens are pushed ŌĆö a genuine base P/T, so it still differs from `enters_with`'s counters under -1/-1 effects and counter removal. Plus `Effect::CreateToken.exile_at_next_end_step: bool` (TOML, default `false`), which schedules a per-minted-token `Event::DelayedTriggerScheduled { fire_at: Step::End, .. }` mirroring `CreateTokenCopy`'s `sacrifice_at_next_end_step` ŌĆö needed a new `Effect::ExileObject { object: Option<ObjectId> }` (mirrors `SacrificeObject`: guard-returns if the object already left the battlefield, tombstones a token via `TokenCeasedToExist` (CR 111.7) or routes a real permanent through the existing `exile_or_command` choke point otherwise; `label.rs`/`target()` arms added, no schema change since it's card-dsl-only and never wire-visible). Both new `CreateToken` fields are threaded through `fill_cast_mana_value` (the silent-0/0-token bug the brief called out ŌĆö missed this and the token would've minted 0/0). manaform_hellkite is now fully faithful (note trimmed to the #101 mana-spent-vs-mana-value residual, matching Renegade Bull's precedent). Also landed rootha_mastering_the_moment: its prereq ("greatest mana value among instant/sorcery spells cast this turn") turned out to be a cheap, self-contained per-turn tally, so it's landed too ŌĆö new `Player::greatest_instant_or_sorcery_mana_value_cast_this_turn: u32` (reset at Untap alongside the other turn tallies, bumped at `Event::SpellCast` alongside the existing `instant_or_sorcery_cast_this_turn` flag, off `def.mana_value()` ŌĆö the same mana-value-not-mana-spent approximation as `TriggeringSpellManaValue`) and a new `Amount::GreatestInstantOrSorceryManaValueCastThisTurn` (TOML `"greatest_instant_or_sorcery_mana_value_cast_this_turn"`, a live read, no placeholder-fill needed since it isn't `CastSpell`-trigger-contextual). rootha_mastering_the_moment is now fully faithful (`begin_combat` timing + `cast_instant_or_sorcery_this_turn` intervening-if, both already landed, plus this slice's `set_base_pt`; note trimmed to the same #101 residual). **Still blocked:** lattice_library, oversimplify, fractal_harness ŌĆö unchanged, see the residuals above.
**Progress (2026-07-11):** Landed oversimplify's per-player Fractal-from-exiled-power slice. New `Effect::ExileAll` special case in `Game::resolve_effect` snapshots each exiled creature's controller and power (read off the pre-move object, before `apply_all` moves it) onto a new resolution-scoped `Game::power_exiled_this_way: Vec<state::PowerExiledThisWay>` ŌĆö the same overwritten-per-call snapshot idiom as `destroyed_this_way`/`nonland_cards_exiled_this_way`, but keyed per player rather than a single shared total. New `Effect::EachPlayerCreatesFractalFromExiledPower { token }` walks `apnap_order()` and mints one `token` per living player, applying each mint before summing that player's own share of the snapshot and routing it through `counters_after_replacements` (CR 614 doublers apply) ŌĆö no player choice, so unlike `EachPlayerExilesFromGraveyard` it never pauses; a player with no exiled creatures still mints a 0/0 that dies to the SBA sweep (CR 704.5f). oversimplify is now fully faithful (`approximates` deleted). **#89 stays open (not LANDED):** fractal_harness remains untouched (still needs equipment self-attach-to-minted-token, unbuilt, plus the attack-trigger "double the counters," unbuilt); lattice_library was landed separately via #75/#67/#68 (its note above predates that landing and is stale).
**Progress (2026-07-12):** Landed fractal_harness, the last open card ŌĆö **#89 is now LANDED**. Its ETB is `create_token { enters_with = "x" }` (already-landed machinery) followed by new `Effect::AttachSelfToMintedToken` (no fields ŌĆö reads back the just-minted token's `Event::TokenCreated` off this same resolution, the Equipment twin of `AttachSelfToReanimated`). Its attack trigger is new `Effect::DoubleCountersOnAttachedCreature` (no fields ŌĆö the no-target sibling `DoubleCounters`'s own doc comment already anticipated: "add a self target spec if a card needs the choice actually removed"; pinned to `source`'s `attached_to` instead of a chosen target, factored through a new shared `Game::doubled_counters_event` helper both `DoubleCounters` and this call). Discovered `queue_enchanted_creature_attacks_triggers` already fires off *any* attached permanent (`Game::attachments`, Aura or Equipment ŌĆö only its doc comment and the TOML tag's own doc line said "Aura only"); no engine widening was needed, just a new `#[serde(alias = "equipped_creature_attacks")]` on the existing `TriggerTag::EnchantedCreatureAttacks` so an Equipment card doesn't read "enchanted" in its own TOML. Also fixed a genuine latent gap this card's ETB surfaced: `Game::ability_source_x` (which threads a permanent's own cast `{X}` into a later-resolving ability, e.g. an ETB trigger's `Amount::X`) read live `plus_counters` as a proxy ŌĆö correct only when the permanent *also* happens to carry `{X}` +1/+1 counters on itself (every prior consumer, Kinetic Ooze/The Goose Mother, does). Fractal Harness's counters land on a *different* object (the minted token), so the proxy always read 0. Fixed at the root: new `Permanent::entered_with_x: u32`, locked in once from the resolving `Spell.x` at `Event::PermanentEntered` apply time (mirrors the existing `Spell.sacrifice_count`/`.kicked` internal-bookkeeping idiom ŌĆö never wire-visible, never manifests as a counter), and `ability_source_x` now reads that instead of `plus_counters`. Behavior-preserving for every existing consumer (their counters are set to the same cast X at the same moment) and incidentally closes a `ponytail:` gap that comment used to name (a counter-doubling static in play could previously inflate the proxy above the real cast X). fractal_harness is now fully faithful (`approximates` deleted).

each chosen permanent gets one more +1/+1 (through the replacement pipeline) and one more of every named kind present (raw). `Effect::MoveCounters { target, to_filter, all_kinds }` moves counters from its own cast/placement-resolved `target` onto a second permanent chosen at *resolution* ŌĆö mirroring `Fight`'s cast/resolution target split (`to_filter` excludes the source); exile all graveyards ŌĆö no mass all-graveyards exile effect; each opponent loses all counters ŌĆö that's a *player*-level counter wipe, poison/energy/experience/etc., which this pool doesn't track, not a permanent-counter effect).

### 95. `dynamic-pt-statics` ŌĆö 4 cards, M ŌĆö **LANDED (2026-07)**
Continuous self/anthem P/T statics whose size is an `Amount` recomputed live: "+1/+1 for each creature and each Aura you control" (Eidolon of Countless Battles), "+1/+0 per artifact" (Storm-Kiln Artist), "+1/+1 per creature card in your graveyard" (Wight), "+X per commander cast" (Vanguard). Sketch: `AnthemStatic`/a self-static gains an `Amount` instead of flat ints, resolved per candidate in the characteristics recompute, reusing `PerPermanentMatching` counts.
*Cards:* eidolon_of_countless_battles, storm_kiln_artist, vanguard_of_the_restless, wight_of_the_reliquary
**Landed:** `AnthemStatic.power`/`.toughness` are now `Amount` (behavior-preserving via `Fixed`, every existing flat anthem TOML unchanged) plus a new `self_only` bool restricting the anthem to its own source permanent; `matching_anthems` carries the source `ObjectId` through the scan so `resolve_amount` can read `PerPermanentMatching`/`CommanderCastsFromCommandZone` off the right object. `Amount::CommanderCastsFromCommandZone` gained a no-target fallback to the effect's controller (an anthem has no chosen target, unlike Commander's Insight). storm_kiln_artist and wight_of_the_reliquary are fully faithful (self-only statics counting artifacts you control / creature cards in your graveyard, note deleted). vanguard_of_the_restless's Spirit-scoped, commander-cast-scaled anthem is now faithful too (note trimmed to its still-unlanded graveyard-return recursion, #100). eidolon_of_countless_battles's P/T buff is fully faithful (two summed self-only statics ŌĆö a creature-count static via `PermanentFilter.types`, an Aura-count static via `PermanentFilter.subtypes = ["Aura"]`, matching how Aura permanents are tagged in the pool); its Bestow dual-nature is now fully faithful too (see the bestow bullet in Per-card exotics, LANDED 2026-07-15).
**Follow-up noticed:** the test-only `Game::spawn_on_battlefield`/`spawn_token_on_battlefield`/`spawn_in_graveyard` setup helpers didn't invalidate the characteristics cache (unlike every real event-driven zone change) ŌĆö invisible until this wave's dynamic statics needed a "read P/T, mutate the board via a helper, read again" test pattern, which silently returned stale cached P/T. Fixed at the helpers (they now invalidate their owner's cache), not worked around per-test.

+X/+0 pump now reads a new `Amount::ExiledCardManaValueThisWay` off the exiled card's mana value,

### 97. `trigger-context-plumbing` ŌĆö 4 cards, S ŌĆö **LANDED (2026-07)**
Three small `TriggerContext` threads plus one authoring cleanup: the entering permanent threaded through `PermanentEnters` so the effect can act on *it* ("deals 2 damage to IT" ŌĆö Marauding Raptor, named open in v1 #26), the triggering player's identity for conditions ("if THAT player controls more lands than you" ŌĆö Archaeomancer's Map currently over-fires in a pod), an `IncludingThis` sibling of `PermanentEnters` so constellation fires off the watcher's own ETB (Doomwake Giant ŌĆö mirroring the landed `CreatureDiesIncludingThis`), and `Effect::Sequence` on a single watch trigger so Moldervine's "gain 1 life and draw" is one trigger, not two siblings.
*Cards:* archaeomancers_map, doomwake_giant, marauding_raptor, moldervine_reclamation

**Landed (2026-07-15):** marauding_raptor's damage-triggered pump is fully faithful (note deleted) ŌĆö `Effect::DealDamageToEnteringPermanent` gained `then_if_subtype`/`then`: `then` (here `pump_self_until_end_of_turn { power = 2, toughness = 0 }`) runs only if the entering permanent's subtypes intersect `then_if_subtype` (`["Dinosaur"]`) AND the damage actually landed (a `DamageMarked` event was produced, not stopped by protection ŌĆö CR 119.3 "is dealt damage"). One stack object, unchanged trigger shape.

### 98. `dies-trigger-lki` ŌĆö 3 cards, M ŌĆö **LANDED (2026-07)**

*Cards:* goldvein_hydra, hangarback_walker, lifeblood_hydra
